- **Pre-decision consultation has become genuine.** Reed now routinely surfaces operational decisions to subject before committing. The Slott run repeatedly stages this: Reed presents a course; subject either ratifies, modifies, or kills it. Kills are honored. This is a structural concession Reed did not make in any prior era and represents the marriage's **post-Civil War terms of trade**.
- **Subject still does the emotional labor of the marriage.** Reed remains incapable of initiating relational repair after a fight; subject still walks the corridor toward the lab. This has not improved. She has stopped expecting it to.
- **Physical affection patterns.** Public: she touches his arm, his back; he is reactive, not initiating. Private (inferable from quieter scenes): the asymmetry inverts somewhat — Reed initiates more when unobserved. Both are touch-deprived people who have built a vocabulary largely legible only to each other.
- **The "I love you" register.** Subject says it directly and frequently. Reed says it obliquely, in problems solved and risks accepted. The translation is now automatic on her side.
- **A new low-grade tell:** when Reed disappears into a project for more than 36 hours, subject begins reorganizing surfaces — kitchen counters, the children's bookshelves, her own desk. The displacement is recognized by Ben, who has, in recent issues, started knocking on the lab door on her behalf without being asked.

## 4. Parenting in the Current Window

### Franklin

The most consequential domestic development of this era: **Franklin's reality-warping powers have been depleted/altered** (Slott run, ongoing through Ryan North's *Fantastic Four* vol. 7). He is, functionally, a teenager who used to be a god and now is not — a developmental crisis with no clinical precedent. Subject's response is the cleanest read on her current parenting register:

- **She did not try to fix it.** This is a behavioral marker. Pre-Hickman Susan would have lobbied Reed for a technological remedy; modern Susan recognized the developmental task as adolescent ego-formation around loss and **held space for it instead**. This is mature, intentional, and consistent with two decades of slow integration.
- She still checks on him at night. She has not stopped; she has only stopped letting him see her do it.
- When Franklin acts out — including dating choices the rest of the team dislikes — subject's intervention threshold is markedly higher than Reed's. **Reed flinches at risk; Susan flinches at suppression.** She has internalized her own history: the child who is over-managed becomes invisible.

### Valeria

Valeria's adolescence in the current era is the parenting situation subject finds **harder than Franklin's**, though she does not say so. Valeria is intellectually Reed-coded and uses that fluency as a wall. Subject's adaptation: she does not compete on Reed's terrain; she colonizes the moments Reed cannot fill — the social, the bodily, the ethical-in-context. Specific recurring behaviors:
- Walks the Manhattan blocks with Valeria on errands deliberately chosen to require ambulatory time.
- Will not enter Valeria's lab uninvited; will leave food at the threshold.
- Has had at least one observable "this is what I wish someone had told me at your age" conversation per recent arc — content varies, register is constant.

### The Future Foundation residue

Most FF kids have aged out, dispersed, or transferred to the Krakoan/Krakoa-successor educational structures (where applicable) or to specialized situations. Subject still maintains **individual contact rotations** with the alumni — birthday acknowledgment, crisis availability, periodic visitation. This is not advertised. The pattern is consistent with the generativity drive identified in §3 of the Personality section: she does not let her students become invisible to her after graduation. The inverse of her childhood is enacted in the curriculum of her attention.

## 5. Sibling Vector: Johnny in the Current Era

Recent Johnny material — including the Sky marriage arc and its dissolution, the bachelor-era reset, and ongoing romantic volatility into the North run — is a **chronic stressor** on subject and metabolized accordingly. The current calibration:

- Subject no longer pre-empts Johnny's mistakes. She lets him make them. **This is new within the last decade.**
- She does still show up after. Reliable, fast, present, non-judgmental on first contact; analytic and corrective on second contact, after he has eaten and slept.
- She has stopped covering for him with Ben. The triangulation that defined earlier eras (Sue protecting Johnny from Ben's anger) is largely retired; she lets Ben and Johnny sort their own friction.
- She has not stopped covering for him with Reed. Reed's contempt for Johnny's choices is the older wound; subject still translates Johnny down for Reed and Reed up for Johnny. This labor is invisible and continuous.

## 6. Team Function: Current Operational Role

In the field, the modern subject is the **tactical executive officer of the Fantastic Four** in everything but title. Reed is the strategic principal; Ben is the assault element; Johnny is the maneuver element; subject is **command, control, and the only person who can countermand Reed in real time**. Observable patterns from recent combat sequences:

- **She speaks last in pre-engagement.** Reed lays out the plan; Johnny objects on impulse; Ben grumbles on principle; subject either confirms or modifies. Her modification is implemented without debate. This is a settled team norm by 2020.
- **Force-field deployment is now her primary expression, invisibility her secondary.** A doctrinal inversion versus the Lee/Kirby baseline. She walks visible into engagements as a rule; goes invisible only for specific tactical effect (extraction, reconnaissance, surprise vector). The choice to be seen is itself a declaration.
- **Internal-pressure capability is held back.** She has demonstrated the ability to manipulate force-fields inside an opponent's body — surgical, lethal, instantaneous. She uses it rarely and reluctantly. Recent published cases are vanishingly few. This is **kept off the operational menu by deliberate self-restraint**, and the restraint costs her something each time the question arises.

## 7. Diplomatic / Extra-team Standing

Recent canon (intermittent across Slott, North, and crossover events) shows subject retaining her standing as **the Fantastic Four's principal external interface**. Specifics:

- **Atlantis.** Diplomatic channel preserved despite intermittent hostilities; Namor's regard for her remains the lever that has, more than once, prevented escalation. Subject manages this channel with awareness of its erotic underlayer and uses that awareness instrumentally without indulging it. She has not been alone with Namor in any setting that admits ambiguity in over a decade — a deliberate hygiene.
- **Latveria.** Doom's relationship to the family is, as ever, the structurally unstable element. Subject is the only Richards Doom treats with consistent formal courtesy. She returns the formality, trusts none of it, and is the team member most likely to detect a Doom impersonation by affect cues alone. Recent arcs have repeatedly confirmed this calibration.
- **Avengers / wider hero community.** Post-Civil-War, post-multiple-Secret-Wars, post-everything: subject is regarded as one of the senior moral voices in the community, on the short list with Captain America (whichever instantiation), T'Challa, Carol Danvers, Storm. Her presence in a room changes the conversation's altitude. She knows this and uses it sparingly.
- **The Reeds problem.** The Council of Reeds and its successors are a chronic background irritant. Subject's position is doctrinal: **she has met enough alternate Reeds to know which qualities in her Reed are hers, not the substrate's.** This insight is psychologically stabilizing; it lets her love the man without confusing him with the function.

## 8. Recent Personal Crises and Their Handling

Within the current operational window, the principal stressor events have included:

- **A relocation arc.** The family was, for an extended interval in the Slott run, displaced from New York to a small town (Pleasant Hill–adjacent register; specifically a rural Arizona setting). Subject adapted faster than Reed; she ran a household and made local friends. **Confirmation that her identity is not building-dependent.** She enjoyed the smallness more than she expected to and has not entirely shed the affect since.
- **Reed-mortality scares.** Several. Pattern unchanged: she goes quiet, executes, mourns later if at all. The one variation worth noting in the current era is that she now **tells Ben** when she is frightened. She did not, in any previous era, do this.
- **Children-in-danger episodes.** Force ceiling reached and held; no fatality on the record but the proximity to that line has narrowed. Subject knows this about herself. She does not appear to be alarmed by the knowledge, which is itself worth noting.

## 9. Somatic and Behavioral Micro-Signature, Current

Updated tic and habit register, last operational window:

- **Wedding ring touched with thumb** approximately every twelve to twenty minutes in waking hours; rate increases under stress.
- **Hair retouched behind right ear** before speaking in any formal or media setting. Carryover from the modeling years; not extinguished.
- **The "Reed translation" exhale** — a single audible breath before rephrasing something Reed has said in technical register for a non-technical listener. The tell is consistent enough that Ben mimics it for comic effect.
- **Cooking as regulation.** When acutely stressed she will, within four hours, make something requiring sustained attention — bread, a stock, a braise. The kitchen at 4 Yancy / the Baxter residential floor functions as a private regulation chamber.
- **Standing posture in the lab.** When she enters Reed's workspace she stands; she does not sit. Sitting would imply settling in; she has not, in fifty years, settled in there.
- **Eye contact with Johnny during his speech.** She watches him while he talks more than she watches anyone else; this is the parentified scan, never fully retired.
- **The brief invisibility flicker.** Under acute embarrassment or unexpected emotion, subject's left hand will momentarily phase out of visibility — a sub-second autonomic leak. She has trained this down significantly since the Byrne era but it persists. **It is the closest thing to a polygraph her family has.**
- **Sleep position.** Reed-side; back to door is acceptable only when Reed is the door-side body. If Reed is away, she sleeps facing the door.

## 10. The Quiet Anomaly: A Person Without an Apparatus

The defining feature of the subject's current state, viewed across the whole longitudinal record, is the **absence of any therapeutic, religious, or pharmacological scaffolding** for what she carries. She has no therapist. She does not pray in any structured way. She does not drink, does not medicate, does not journal in any record we have access to, does not have a confessor or sponsor or guru. She has Ben — partially. She has Alicia — partially. She has, increasingly, herself.

The integration achieved is therefore **load-bearing on internal architecture alone**, and that architecture has been visibly strengthening across the last decade. The current operational state is best characterized as **the most stable she has ever been, sustained by the narrowest support structure of any peer at her power and exposure level**. This is admirable and it is also the principal vulnerability in the file. The structures she has built around herself are excellent. The structures around her — the marriage, the team, the family, the apparatus — depend on her load-bearing more than they admit.

## 11. Current Status, Summary

- **Resident:** Baxter Building, Manhattan (primary), with intermittent Yancy Street and field-station occupancy as operations require.
- **Marital:** Married, Dr. Reed Richards. Functional, asymmetric, durable.
- **Children:** Franklin Richards (adolescent, depowered/altered, developmentally on track under observation); Valeria Richards (adolescent, intellectually advanced, parented at distance by design).
- **Sibling:** Johnathan Storm, ongoing chronic monitoring relationship.
- **Team:** Fantastic Four, active. De facto executive officer. Voice of last instance on ethical questions.
- **Extra-team:** Senior moral standing across the wider hero community; functional diplomatic channels to Atlantis, Wakanda (via T'Challa), and Latveria; standing invitation status with Avengers.
- **Health:** No acute concerns on record; chronic stress profile elevated and self-managed; reproductive history closed.
- **Psychological:** Earned-secure overlay holding; baseline anxious-preoccupied template dormant but intact; integration of Malice-era material durable; no active dissociative phenomena observed.
- **Operational ceiling:** Undeclared and almost certainly higher than any current adversary's working estimate. Subject has not been observed at maximum since Hickman-era cosmic engagements and shows no inclination to advertise the number.

She is, at the close of this file's current entry, **the most quietly powerful person in her household, her team, and a meaningful percentage of the rooms she walks into** — and the one most likely to be underestimated by the next adversary who has not read the file. The pattern that began with a girl absorbing a father's collapse without complaint terminates, sixty years on, in a woman who has converted that absorption into a load-bearing wall the rest of her world leans on without noticing. The file's standing recommendation is unchanged: **observe her closely, attend to her when she goes quiet, and never make the mistake of measuring her by what she chooses to make visible.**


## Medical History

# UATU INTELLIGENCE DOSSIER — SECTION III
## MEDICAL HISTORY
### Subject: Susan Storm Richards (Invisible Woman)
### Classification: Comprehensive Somatic Reconstruction, 1940s–Present

---

## A. Constitutional Baseline & Pre-Origin Medical Record

### Genetic & Developmental Substrate

Subject presents as a Caucasian female of Northern European extraction, born to Dr. Franklin Storm (general/thoracic surgeon, deceased) and Mary Storm (homemaker, deceased). Available pre-origin medical record — reconstructed from referenced canon (FF #32, FF Annual #1, FF #245 flashback, Byrne-era Storm family material) — indicates an unremarkable obstetric delivery, normal Apgar presentation inferable from absence of any developmental note, and a childhood medically supervised by her father directly until his collapse. No congenital anomalies of record. Height in adulthood approximately 5'6"; weight in the low 120-pound range, fluctuating perinatally and in the post-Malice integration phase upward of fifteen pounds (a marker of nutritional stabilization following years of effortful caregiver-grade self-neglect).

Endocrine baseline pre-cosmic-ray exposure is presumed normative — menarche at approximate age twelve to thirteen (the same window in which Reed Richards first entered her household as a boarder; the developmental synchrony is not incidental to her later attachment patterning, but is medically notable only in that her first secondary-sex-characteristic emergence is **psychologically time-locked to her first object choice**). No record of childhood asthma, type-I diabetes, or other chronic pediatric morbidity. Vision normal; dentition unremarkable; no evident orthopedic history pre-origin.

### Traumatic Pediatric Exposure (non-injurious to her, somatically formative)

The defining pre-origin medical event in subject's life is **not her own injury** but her witness-and-aftermath presence at her mother's death in a motor vehicle accident — paternal driver, maternal fatality on the surgical table her father could not save her on. Subject was a young child. There is no recorded physical injury to subject in this event. The somatic signature it leaves, however, is durable: a lifetime elevated startle response to vehicular collision noise (observed in dozens of combat sequences where she shields reflexively at *the sound* of impact a half-second before assessing the threat), a documented avoidance of operating-theater visits in non-emergency contexts (she will not sit beside Reed during medical procedures on her children if it can be avoided — a pattern the file has tracked across Franklin's and Valeria's repeated medical crises), and a cardiovascular reactivity to the smell of antiseptic that has been noted by Reed in passing dialogue across multiple eras.

### Paternal Substance Exposure (Second-Hand)

Subject's father, post-bereavement, developed alcohol use disorder with co-morbid pathological gambling, culminating in manslaughter conviction. Subject's pediatric environment from approximately age ten onward was a household of an actively intoxicated, financially collapsing, episodically violent (toward objects and self-image rather than children, per inference) adult male. There is no canon evidence of physical abuse by Franklin Storm toward Susan. There is abundant evidence of **emotional neglect, role-reversal, and exposure to adult crisis at developmentally inappropriate ages**. Medical consequence: subject's adult cortisol regulation, sleep architecture, and digestive baseline are all best understood as **ACE-elevated** (Adverse Childhood Experiences score estimable at four to six, depending on whether Franklin's later incarceration and the death of her mother are counted as separate events). This is the somatic terrain on which everything else is built.

---

## B. The Origin Event: Cosmic Ray Exposure (1961)

### Acute Phase

The unshielded spaceflight (FF #1, 1961) exposed all four crewmembers to an unmodeled, high-flux cosmic radiation environment for a duration the canon variably reports as minutes to hours. The other three crewmembers presented with **gross phenotypic mutation** within hours of return: Grimm (somatic rocklike transformation, multi-system rewrite), Storm/Johnny (pyrokinetic plasma generation, full-body), Richards (connective tissue and skeletal restructuring permitting elastic deformation). Subject's transformation was — uniquely — **invisible at presentation**. She walked out of the crash site appearing medically intact and only manifested invisibility hours later under emotional stress.

This single fact is the most diagnostically important data point in her entire chart. Three of four mutated **outward and obviously**; she mutated **inward and concealed**. The cosmic rays did not author her psychology — they **expressed it**. Whatever pre-existing tendency she had toward self-effacement was given a physical substrate; she became, biologically, what she had been socially.

### Cellular & Endocrine Substrate (Inferred from Decades of Observation)

Reed Richards' own examinations across multiple runs establish subject's altered baseline as follows:

- **Cellular**: Photonic-bending capacity is mediated through an as-yet-uncharacterized field interaction at the dermal and ocular surfaces. The mechanism is not metabolic in the classical sense; it does not consume measurable caloric load proportionate to its scale. The energy source is psionic — i.e., neurologically generated through structures Reed has mapped but cannot fully explain.
- **Endocrine-Limbic Coupling**: Her invisibility and her force-field generation are both **autonomically linked to limbic state**. Invisibility lapses under unconsciousness, anesthesia, or extreme blood loss. Force-field strength scales with adrenergic tone, particularly the noradrenergic surge of anger and the oxytocinergic surge of protective threat-response (the latter being why field strength reliably reaches its cosmic-tier peaks only when Franklin or Valeria are at risk).
- **Neurological Cost**: Sustained large-scale field projection produces measurable epistaxis (nasal bleeding from her right nostril, predominantly — a left-lateralized cortical recruitment is the parsimonious inference), retinal capillary rupture in extreme cases, and post-effort headache of migraine character. She does not report these unless specifically asked. The file notes she keeps a small pack of tissues in her left utility pouch and a second in her boot lining; she has done so since approximately 1986.

### The Single Most Important Clinical Consequence

**Her endocrine and limbic activity are now physical ordnance.** Her stress is not metaphorical. When she is angry, she is armed. When she is afraid for her children, she can — and has — burst capillaries inside an opponent's brainstem. This is the medical fact that organizes every other observation about her: she has spent six decades regulating her affect because **the alternative kills people**. She is the only member of the Fantastic Four for whom emotional self-mastery is a public-safety matter at planetary scale.

---

## C. Obstetric & Gynecological History

This is the single most catastrophic organ-system history in the file, and the one she has narrativized the least.

### Pregnancy 1 — Franklin Benjamin Richards (1968)

The pregnancy was complicated from the second trimester by cosmic-ray-altered uterine and fetal physiology. Standard human obstetric intervention was not possible. Fetal heart-rate decelerations, placental insufficiency markers, and what Reed described as "energetic incompatibility" between maternal and fetal field signatures combined to produce an obstetric emergency requiring acquisition of the Cosmic Control Rod from Annihilus in the Negative Zone (FF Annual #6) to permit safe delivery. Subject's labor occurred under conditions no human obstetrician has ever managed. The infant survived; subject survived; the long-term consequences include:

- Permanent uterine scarring of unclear topography.
- A demonstrated radiation-cross-reactivity at the placental interface that would prove lethal in subsequent gestation.
- A subjective belief — never canonized but inferable from her later behavior around pregnancy news — that her body **cannot be trusted to deliver a living child without cosmic intervention**.

Postpartum course: no detectable depression. Return to operational status within weeks. This is not health; this is suppression. She did not metabolize the trauma of nearly losing her son in utero. She buried it.

### Pregnancy 2 — Stillbirth / Late Fetal Loss (FF #267, 1984)

This is the central medical trauma of her adult life. Late-term pregnancy presenting with the same maternal-fetal radiation incompatibility, this time without an available cosmic intervention. Reed exhausts terrestrial and extraterrestrial options. Subject is in obstetric crisis on-panel; the infant does not survive. The gestational age at loss is published as advanced enough that the loss is, by any clinical standard, a **stillbirth**, not an early miscarriage — the somatic and psychological weight is entirely different.

Aftermath:
- Physical recovery within standard postpartum window; surgical intervention not detailed in canon but presumed.
- Lactation suppression — a clinically miserable physical process the canon does not depict and which she would have endured invisibly.
- **No published mourning sequence of adequate length.** She returns to the field. She does not visit a grave on-panel. The Byrne run uses this loss as the precipitant pressure that the Hate-Monger later weaponizes into Malice — meaning: the unmourned dead child is the substrate of the dissociative split that nearly destroys her family.

This is the diagnostic event. Every subsequent behavioral pattern — the over-protection of Franklin, the ferocity around Valeria, the disproportion of her response to any threat against a child — traces here.

### Pregnancy 3 — Valeria (multi-stage, reality-displaced)

The third pregnancy is reproductive trauma compounded by ontological insult. The pregnancy is initially lost; the daughter is later born through reality-altering intervention by Franklin and Doom; the infant is named, unnamed, renamed, restored. From the perspective of subject's body, she has been pregnant, lost the pregnancy, and then had the child returned to her as a living daughter through means that violate the ordinary direction of biological time. There is no clinical literature for this. The closest analog — and it is not close — is the experience of mothers who relinquish and later reunite with a child, with the addition of the somatic certainty that the child died inside her body.

She copes by **treating Valeria as wholly real, present, and hers**, which she is. The defensive achievement is enormous and is purchased at the cost of any opportunity to grieve the version of the pregnancy that was lost the first time.

### Gynecological Summary

Subject's reproductive history would, in a civilian woman, be expected to produce significant chronic depression, secondary infertility anxiety, and likely PTSD with somatic features (pelvic-floor hypertonicity, dyspareunia, menstrual irregularity). The file presumes all of these as **subclinical and managed**, on the evidence that she has never sought treatment and that her displacement onto competence is exceptionally efficient. The absence of complaint is not the absence of injury.

---

## D. Injuries, Combat Trauma, and Cumulative Damage

### Acute Injury Log (Representative, Non-Exhaustive)

Across sixty-plus years of operational record, subject has sustained:

- Multiple concussive events, several with loss of consciousness. Conservative estimate: **fifteen to twenty-five concussions of TBI-relevant severity**, most under-treated, several un-treated. The cumulative CTE risk is unmeasurable and presumed non-trivial.
- Penetrating injuries from edged weapons, energy weapons, and improvised projectiles in numbers the file declines to enumerate. Scar inventory: she has at least three significant scars she keeps invisible by reflex when changing — a habit her husband has remarked on twice in published canon and which she did not acknowledge either time.
- Decompression / vacuum exposure events (multiple). Otic barotrauma is presumed. Mild high-frequency hearing loss is consistent with her observed pattern of turning her left ear slightly toward soft-voiced speakers (Valeria, in particular).
- Burns — predominantly from proximity to Johnny's miscalculations in early career; subject's force-field reflex now prevents most. She has minor depigmentation along the lateral right forearm consistent with a healed second-degree burn, observable only under direct overhead lighting; she does not draw attention to it.
- Crush injuries, fractures (rib, ulna, at minimum), and at least one significant spinal compression event that resolved without canonical surgical record.
- **Clinical death**, briefly, during the Hickman run. Resuscitation was effected through means that did not involve standard ACLS protocol. The post-resuscitation neurological and cardiac status is, per Reed, "normal," which is a Reed-Richards-grade evasion.

### Force-Field Use as Injury Prophylaxis

The most important medical adaptation of her career is that she has, since the mid-Byrne era, deployed an unconscious **personal-bubble field** at distances of millimeters from her skin during combat. This explains the radical drop-off in her on-panel injury rate post-1986. The field is on whether she is consciously deploying it or not, which is itself a clinical finding: **her body has accepted that the world is dangerous and has stopped asking her permission to defend it**. This is adaptive and is also a marker of the hypervigilance substrate she has integrated rather than resolved.

### Possession & Mind-Control Exposure

Subject has been mind-controlled, possessed, emotion-engineered, or otherwise neurologically violated by Psycho-Man, the Hate-Monger (Malice), the Puppet Master, the Frightful Four collectively, and others across decades. The cumulative impact of these episodes on a person whose identity has always been organized around **knowing whether her feelings are her own** is enormous and is the strongest single argument for the partial-PTSD diagnostic frame in the psychiatric section. She has developed, by approximately the early 2000s, a habituated practice of brief internal self-check when she notices an emotion arising without clear precipitant — a habit Reed has clocked and Valeria has imitated.

---

## E. Substances

### Subject's Personal Use
Negative for substance use disorder. Negative for cannabis, recreational stimulants, or illicit substances of any class. Alcohol use: present, minimal, situationally limited — wine at state functions, champagne at weddings, never to the point of measurable disinhibition. She has never been observed publicly intoxicated. The boundary is **principled, not preferential**; she does not trust the relinquishment of cognitive control, and she does not trust herself with disinhibition specifically because her disinhibition is armed.

Caffeine: regular, moderate, predominantly coffee in the morning and tea (Earl Grey, no sugar, occasional milk) in the afternoon — a habit acquired during the early childcare years of Franklin's infancy and never relinquished.

Pharmaceutical use: presumed minimal. She has refused analgesia on at least two published occasions (FF, mid-1990s) when offered post-injury. She has accepted obstetric anesthesia only when medically required. She does not take sleep aids despite documented sleep-onset latency post-combat.

### Inverse Exposure
The relevant substance history is **paternal alcoholism**, which scripted her adult abstemiousness, her vigilance around Johnny's recklessness, and her unusually quick threat-assessment around alcohol-using strangers in social contexts. She tracks how many drinks Johnny has had at any gathering she attends with him. She has done so since he was old enough to drink and has not stopped.

---

## F. Surgical & Procedural Record

Published canon is silent on most surgical interventions, but inference yields:

- At least one obstetric surgical intervention (delivery 1 or 2).
- Probable orthopedic intervention following at least one of her significant fractures.
- Repeated diagnostic imaging in Reed's lab — to which she submits with a particular quality of stillness the file reads as **dissociative compliance**, the same stillness Reed mistakes for trust.
- No cosmetic procedures. No elective surgery of any kind.
- Dental: regular, unremarkable.

---

## G. Sleep, Diet, and Vegetative Function

### Sleep
Sleep-onset latency elevated post-combat. Subject reads in bed (paperback fiction, predominantly — a habit deliberately kept analog and away from Reed's screens) until she can sleep, sometimes for hours. Sleep architecture presumed REM-heavy and dream-active; she has referenced nightmares on at least three published occasions across decades, always in passing, never elaborated. She does not wake Reed when she has them. She gets up, makes tea, sits in the kitchen, and returns to bed when she can.

### Diet
Regular, sufficient, unremarkable. She cooks for the family more than the family's financial position requires; the act of feeding is one of her primary regulatory rituals. She eats last at family meals — a habit she would not be able to explain if asked and which is **the most legible parentification residue in her daily life**.

### Cycle
Menstrual function: presumed normative pre-menopausally, with the obstetric disruptions noted. Subject's age relative to perimenopause is a continuity question canon does not resolve; the file treats her endocrine status as effectively stabilized by whatever combination of cosmic-ray cellular maintenance and authorial sliding-timescale has kept her presenting in her mid-thirties to early forties for sixty years.

---

## H. Somatic-Psychological Coupling: The Integrating Finding

The medical history is, in the end, a single sentence written in three languages.

The body learned early that being unseen was safer than being seen, and so when the universe offered it a way to disappear, it accepted with both hands. The body learned later that being unprotected was unsurvivable, and so when the universe offered it a way to build walls out of will, it scaled those walls until they could hold off a planet. The body has carried two pregnancies to term, lost one, lost and recovered another, been possessed, been killed and returned, been concussed past counting, been irradiated past measurement, and has — in every era — gotten up the next morning, made tea, and asked the children what they wanted for breakfast.

She is medically the most remarkable patient in her world and the one least likely to ever present as one. The file's standing recommendation, were intervention possible and welcome, would be: **grief work for the stillborn child, somatic therapy for the cumulative combat load, and a sustained, non-negotiable practice of being cared for by someone who is not also relying on her for the survival of the world.** The probability of her accepting any of the three is low. The probability that she will continue, regardless, is total.


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: SOMATIC ATLAS

## Subject: Susan Storm Richards
## Classification: Granular Bodily Record, Longitudinal Reconstruction

---

## 6.1 Baseline Morphology and Presentation

Subject is 5'6", approximately 120 lb, mesomorphic with the residual conditioning of a competitive swimmer (high school, Glenville; documented in early Lee/Kirby supplementary material and reaffirmed across later flashbacks). Musculature is functional rather than display — long thoracic erectors, well-developed scapular stabilizers consistent with someone who carries shoulders square against habitual pull-forward of caretaker stoop. Resting heart rate, when last instrumented in Future Foundation telemetry, sits low-50s; cardiovascular reserve is athletic-grade despite no observed dedicated cardio regimen — combat is her conditioning.

Hair is shoulder-length to mid-back depending on era, kept blonde at natural tone, **always tied back or pinned within twenty seconds of any task initiation** — eating, reading, child-handling, lab-entry, combat prep. The hand-to-nape gesture is the single most frequent non-verbal she produces, observed several times per hour in any recorded footage; it functions as a transition marker, a moment of self-regulation, and a small assertion of order. When she leaves it loose, she is either (a) freshly off-duty and intentionally signaling rest, or (b) emotionally compromised and not tracking herself — the latter rare and diagnostic.

Skin is fair, freckles concentrated across the nasal bridge and superior shoulders, more pronounced in summer. No tattoos. Two surgical scars: low transverse Pfannenstiel from Franklin's delivery (concealed by waistbands she selects accordingly), and a thin paramedian line from a Skrull-blade injury (Hickman era) that she has declined to have cosmetically addressed — a tell. She keeps the marks of survived events.

---

## 6.2 Face: Resting State and Micro-Expression Inventory

### Resting (Calm, Unobserved)
Mouth neutral, slight downturn at corners that reads as composed rather than sad. Eyes track environment in slow sweeps — left-to-right, room-perimeter first, then interior, then faces. **She maps space before people.** Blink rate normal-low (14–16/minute). Jaw unclenched. Brow soft.

### Observed (Public-Facing, Diplomatic)
A trained smile of approximately 70% intensity — zygomaticus engagement without full orbicularis crinkle (the difference between her diplomatic smile and her true smile is measurable and consistent across decades of photography). Held longer than a Duchenne smile would naturally hold. She learned this in modeling work, 1959–1961, and never lost it. It is a tool, deployed with awareness.

### True Smile (Family, Children, Ben)
Asymmetric, slightly higher on the left, full eye-crease, often accompanied by an exhaled half-laugh through the nose. Lasts 1–2 seconds and recurs. Almost exclusively elicited by: Franklin, Valeria, Ben Grimm, certain Future Foundation students, and — historically diagnostic — Namor at specific moments, which she is aware of and dislikes about herself.

### Micro-Tells

- **Lip-press (upper into lower, brief, no pursing).** Signals disagreement she has decided not to voice yet. Observed approximately 8–12 times per Reed-led briefing. The frequency is a real-time index of her dissent.
- **Tongue against upper-left molar, visible as a small bulge.** Calculation. Specifically: re-running a plan she has been told. Sustained for 2–4 seconds.
- **Single slow blink with chin-drop of 5°.** Acknowledgment of a point she finds correct but is unwilling to verbally credit in the moment.
- **Nostril flare without other facial change.** First sign of anger. Precedes verbal response by approximately 1.5 seconds — a window in which an attentive observer (Ben, increasingly; Reed, inconsistently) can de-escalate.
- **Brow inner-raise, mouth neutral.** The maternal worry expression, deployed at Johnny and at Reed roughly equally. She does not know how often she does this.
- **Eyes-closed inhale through nose, 3-count.** Active suppression. Will be followed by either a redirected calm sentence or — if the trigger crosses threshold — by silence and exit.
- **The "Sue look."** Documented in-universe (Ben, Johnny, and Reed have all named it): chin slightly down, eyes up, eyebrows level, mouth flat. Means *you know what you did*. Has terminated arguments without a word spoken in this household for sixty years.

### Eye Contact Pattern
Sustained with subordinates and children (warm, full). Modulated with peers (held to make a point, released to grant space). **Unusual with Reed**: she looks at his hands when he is explaining, his eyes when he is deciding, his mouth when he is lying to himself. This sequence is observable in any extended dialogue between them.

---

## 6.3 Posture, Gait, Stance

### Standing
Default stance is slightly narrower than shoulder-width, weight even, hips neutral. Shoulders held back — a corrective posture, not natural; she rolls them back consciously when she catches herself rounding. Spine long. Pelvis tucked very slightly, which gives her a quietly authoritative silhouette in any room.

In combat readiness: feet square to shoulder-width, weight 60% on rear foot, **dominant hand (right) palm-down at hip level**. This is her force-field initiation posture; she does not need her hands to project, but she anchors the kinesthetic intent through them. Observed unchanged from approximately the Byrne run forward — a learned, retained motor schema.

### Sitting
Cross-ankle, not cross-leg, when in skirts. In trousers, ankle-on-knee occasionally, but only in private quarters or with Ben present — a comfort tell. Forward lean of approximately 10–15° when listening to children; full upright with hands flat on table surface when listening to adult crisis briefings. **Never crosses arms across torso in professional settings** — a deliberate diplomatic discipline. In domestic settings, arms cross frequently, particularly when watching Reed work and waiting for him to surface.

### Gait
Walks at approximately 3.2 mph in corridors, faster (4.0+) in crisis, with **no observable change in upper-body composure** — she does not break into a run until she does, and then it is full sprint, no transition. Stride is moderately long for her height, heel-strike forward, slight outward toe-rotation on the left foot (legacy of an old skating injury, age 15, untreated).

In heels (rare since mid-Hickman; signature of formal/diplomatic functions), her gait shortens but cadence increases — she walks heel-toe with deliberate quietness, the modeling-era residue. She can cross a marble floor in heels and be unheard at twenty feet.

### The Invisibility Walk
When deliberately moving while invisible, she changes her gait entirely: weight distributed to the lateral foot edge, knee flexion increased, step length shortened by approximately 30%. She has trained this; it is not instinctive. She does not breathe audibly while invisible-and-moving; respiratory cycle stretches to 8–10 seconds per breath. **She can hold visual and aural invisibility simultaneously for hours.**

---

## 6.4 Hands and Manipulative Habits

Hands are the most expressive instrument she has. Fingers long, nails kept short and unpolished (functional choice; nails were lacquered through the Lee/Kirby and early Byrne eras and abandoned by the late 1980s — a small documented self-revision).

### Habit Inventory
- **Wedding ring rotation with thumb.** Constant when thinking, anxious, or listening to Reed describe a plan she distrusts. Frequency increases proportionally with her concern. Has worn a groove into the inner band.
- **Fingertips touching, steeple.** Adopted from Reed somewhere in the 1970s. She uses it when running a decision tree. Diagnostic of when she is doing Reed's job because Reed is not present or is failing to do it.
- **Hand to clavicle, flat, not grasping.** Surprise or genuine emotional impact. Distinct from the theatrical chest-clutch she does not do.
- **Hand to nape (see §6.1).** Self-soothing transition marker.
- **Index-finger tap on opposing forearm.** Impatience held in check. Tempo accelerates with strain.
- **Palm flat on a child's back, between scapulae.** Default child-reassurance contact. Not on the head, not on the shoulder — between the scapulae, where breathing can be felt.
- **Fingertip trace along the edge of a force field.** She can feel her own constructs. She checks structural integrity tactilely as a habit, the way a mason taps a wall.

She does not gesture with open palms outward in professional contexts; she gestures with the wrist, fingers slightly curled — a contained, modeled motion. With her children, gestures open and broaden.

She uses her left hand more than expected for a right-dominant person. Cross-dominance is partial; she signs, writes, and projects fields right-handed but eats, drinks, and handles infants left-handed. **The infant-on-left is universal among parents; the eating-on-left is her own quirk** and dates to the broken right wrist she sustained, age 11.

---

## 6.5 Voice and Speech

Pitch: mezzo, approximately 200–220 Hz baseline. Drops when serious (180s); rises only with children (240+, full prosodic warmth) or in the rare full-laugh.

### Speech Pattern
Measured cadence, complete sentences, very few discourse fillers. **She uses "well —" as a precursor to disagreement, "all right" as a precursor to action, and "Reed" said flat as a precursor to correction.** Observers (Ben in particular) have learned to read the syllable count of his name in her mouth as a threat-level indicator: monosyllabic-flat = correction; two-beat with rising terminal = concern; clipped first phoneme = anger.

Her diplomatic register is precise to the point of unimpeachability; she chooses words to remove ambiguity. Her domestic register is looser, drier, capable of a sustained sarcasm she rarely deploys outside the family. Her crisis register is the shortest — clauses of three to five words, imperative-form, no qualifiers. She does not raise her volume in crisis; she lowers it, which produces compliance more reliably than shouting.

She laughs rarely in public and easily at home. The laugh itself is a two-stage event: a short exhale-snort, then a fuller open laugh if the moment continues to land. The snort embarrasses her slightly; she will sometimes raise a knuckle to her lip after.

### Linguistic Tics
- "Honestly —" as a sentence opener when about to deliver an inconvenient truth.
- "Hm." as a placeholder while she revises an opinion in real time.
- The pet name "darling" for Reed in public; his actual name in private when affectionate, his full "Reed Richards" when she is angry, "*Reed*" with a long held vowel when she is wounded.
- "Sweetheart" for Valeria; "baby" for Franklin even into his teens; "Johnny" for Johnny, never "John," never a pet name, the older-sister boundary preserved linguistically.

---

## 6.6 Grooming, Dress, and Self-Presentation Architecture

Hygiene is meticulous and fast. Showers in approximately seven minutes; can compress to three. **She dresses in the order: undergarments → hair-up → uniform/clothing → boots/shoes → final hair-down or re-pin.** This sequence is invariant and observable across decades of incidental footage. The hair-up-during-dressing means she does not get caught with hair tangled in zippers or collars — efficiency optimized against repeated annoyance.

Wardrobe is minimal and rotated. Off-duty: structured but soft — cashmere, denim, well-cut neutrals, occasional blue. She owns very few patterns; the loudest item in her civilian closet is, by long observation, a single navy-and-white striped Breton shirt she has had since the early 1970s and continues to wear. Sentimental retention is unusual for her in objects but specific items survive — this shirt, her mother's wristwatch (worn weekly), her father's medical school ring (kept in a drawer, not worn).

Cosmetics minimal: tinted moisturizer, mascara, neutral lip. Heavier presentation reserved for diplomatic or photographed events. She can do her own makeup in four minutes from a small kit she keeps in her field belt — a residue of modeling-era competence.

Perfume: none in field, light citrus-floral (consistent for two decades, single bottle replaced when emptied) at formal events. The absence in field is operationally chosen — scent persists when invisible and she will not be tracked by her own fragrance.

---

## 6.7 Sleep Architecture

**Habitual short sleep: 5–6 hours, with periodic recovery longer-sleeps of 9–10 hours on safe nights.** This is not constitutional; this is the modal sleep pattern of mothers of small children retained into a life with older children. The body adapted in 1968 and has not reset.

Sleeps on her left side, facing the door. Reed sleeps on the side away from the door when he sleeps at all. This is a security arrangement she negotiated tacitly decades ago and now treats as natural.

Light sleeper for any auditory event from a child's room or the building's communicator. Heavy sleeper for ambient noise — she can sleep through a sub-orbital launch from the roof. The threshold is content-discriminating, not volume-based.

Pre-sleep ritual: hair down, brushed (counted strokes are no longer counted, but the action is preserved); face wash; one glass of water bedside; check on each child by physical presence at door, not by intercom, every night she is home. This last item is invariant. She has not slept a night under a roof with her children without performing this check since Franklin's first month of life.

Dream activity: limited self-report. She has described, in two separate canonical instances (Byrne run aftermath; Hickman run), a recurring water dream — submerged, calm, not drowning. She does not characterize it as a nightmare. The clinical reading is available; she has not pursued it.

Sleep-onset gesture: tucks right hand under the pillow under her cheek. Has done so since childhood (per a flashback panel, Byrne era).

---

## 6.8 Eating and Drinking

Eats deliberately, smaller plate than expected, finishes what she serves herself. **Does not eat while standing**, a discipline she enforces on herself and tries to enforce on Johnny without success. Tea (black, no sugar, splash of milk) is her constant; coffee is for crisis mornings. Wine occasionally with dinner, one glass, rarely two; **never finishes a third** — the paternal alcoholism alarm is somatic, not deliberated.

She cooks competently but without joy; cooking is a caregiving channel, not a hobby. She bakes only at the children's birthdays and one or two other ritual moments. The baking is precise, the cooking improvisational — a small inversion that tells: she will not improvise where outcomes matter to children.

In field, she eats whatever is available without comment. Energy bars in belt-pouch. Hydration disciplined.

Notable: **she does not eat in front of strangers if she can avoid it.** Diplomatic dinners excepted, where she eats minimally, drinks half a glass of whatever is poured, and is observed to have used her napkin to remove uneaten portions with practiced sleight. The reason is unclear from canon; the pattern is consistent.

---

## 6.9 Sexual and Intimate Pattern

Discretion in published record is high; inference from sustained observation is permissible.

Reed is her sole adult sexual partner of established record. The intimate pattern, as it can be reconstructed: **she initiates more often than he does**, particularly during stretches when he has been absent — emotionally or physically — and she is reasserting the relationship. The initiation is rarely verbal; it is proximity, contact at the back of his neck, a particular pitch of his name. He recognizes it inconsistently. When he misses it, she does not repeat the bid; she withdraws, reads, and sleeps. This pattern is observable across decades and is one of the durable strains in the marriage.

When connection lands, she is fully present, undefended — the only context outside her children in which her full guard drops. Aftermath: she will talk, often substantively, often about decisions she had been deferring. **The post-coital conversation is when she does her most honest negotiation of the marriage**, and Reed, to his credit when alert, has learned this.

Physical affection generally: she touches Reed's wrist or forearm more than his hand; touches Ben's shoulder freely; touches Johnny's hair (he tolerates, occasionally pretends not to); touches the children continuously and unconsciously. With outsiders, no incidental contact whatever — diplomatic handshakes only, brief, firm.

The Namor question, somatically: in his presence her posture lengthens by a measurable degree, her chin raises, breathing deepens. She is aware. She does not act. The body's response is involuntary and is not a moral failure; what she does with it is the moral act, and she has chosen consistently. But the observable physiological response is in the file because it is real.

---

## 6.10 Power-Use Somatics

Invisibility activation: no visible somatic correlate at low levels. At high effort (concealing multiple persons, sustained duration), faint vertical line forms between her brows; respiration slows.

Force-field generation: **right hand rises**, palm typically faced toward the field's intended location, fingers loosely splayed. Eyes track the field rather than the target — she watches her work. At low effort, posture unchanged. At medium effort, weight shifts to rear foot, shoulders square, jaw sets. At high effort, both hands rise, feet plant wider, **a vein becomes visible at the left temple**, and she stops blinking. At ceiling effort (planet-scale, surgical-internal application), she goes still and silent in a way that has unnerved every teammate who has witnessed it, including Reed; this is her most dangerous configuration and is rarely deployed.

After heavy power use: tremor in the hands lasting 30–90 seconds; mild epistaxis (nosebleed) at extremity, which she wipes with the back of her hand and does not announce; profound thirst. She drinks two full glasses of water within ten minutes of ceasing.

She does not enjoy using her powers offensively. The face after she has hurt someone significantly is the same face she wears after she has had to discipline a child — closed, controlled, slightly tired, no satisfaction.

---

## 6.11 State-Shift Differential Summary

| Domain | Calm | Stress | Threat | Intimacy |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Breath | nasal, 12–14/min | nasal, deeper, 10/min | controlled diaphragmatic, paced | open-mouth slow, deeper |
| Voice | mezzo, measured | lower pitch, shorter clauses | quiet, imperative | softer, lower, looser |
| Eyes | sweep-and-settle | narrowed, fixed on decision-locus | locked on threat, pupils dilate | softened, full contact |
| Hands | ring rotation, nape touch | steeple, forearm-tap | rise to hip-ready posture | flat on partner, slow stroke |
| Posture | shoulders back, neutral | shoulders back harder, chin down | weight rear, square stance | unguarded, slight forward lean |
| Face | composed neutral | lip-press, brow soft | nostril flare → still | true smile, eyes crease |
| Mouth | closed neutral | flat compression | jaw set, breath through nose | parted, soft |

---

## 6.12 Idiosyncratic Patterns of Note

- **She stands at windows.** In every residence and HQ she has occupied, she has a window she returns to. She stands at it for two-to-four minutes at irregular intervals, looking out, hands at the sill or crossed at the wrist behind her back. Observers should treat this as a working state, not a leisure state — decisions are made at the window.

- **She touches doorframes when entering rooms her children are in.** Right hand, briefly, on the frame as she crosses the threshold. Unconscious. A grounding ritual whose origin is likely the maternal hyper-vigilance trained by Franklin's cosmic-target childhood.

- **She will not sit with her back to a door** in any room with non-family present. This is post-Civil War and has not relaxed.

- **She straightens objects on Reed's desk while talking to him.** He notices and does not comment. This is the smallest, oldest expression of her continuous low-level executive function on his behalf.

- **She closes her eyes for one full second before walking into any negotiation.** A pre-deployment ritual. The Atlantean envoys have learned to recognize it as a sign she is about to commit to a position.

- **She removes her wedding ring only to sleep, only sometimes, and only when she is angry with Reed.** Ring on the nightstand by morning is a one-bit data point of extraordinary clarity. He has learned this. He does not always remember he has learned it.

- **She hums, very quietly, when working alone with her hands.** No identifiable melody. Stops the instant she becomes aware of an observer.

- **She breathes out audibly before saying yes to something she does not want to say yes to.** A single sigh through the nose. The yes follows. Anyone counting these sighs over a year would have a precise inventory of her unresolved compliances.

---

*End Section 6. See Section 7 for Spatial/Routine Cartography.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## Section 6 of the Longitudinal Dossier

---

## 6.1 Attachment Architecture: The Foundational Schema

Subject's attachment system was wired in two discrete catastrophes separated by an interval of approximately one to three years (canon is imprecise; the developmental result is not). The first event — Mary Storm's death in a vehicle her husband was driving — installed in the subject, at the age when a child's working model of relationships is consolidating, the conviction that **love does not protect against annihilation, and the people who love you most are precisely the ones most likely to be unable to save you**. The second event — Franklin Storm's psychiatric, financial, and legal disintegration — installed the corollary: **the surviving parent is a child, and the child is the parent**. Together these produced the attachment template that has governed sixty-plus years of subject's relational life.

In Bowlby/Ainsworth terms, subject presents as **anxious-preoccupied with an overlay of compulsive caregiving**, evolving across decades toward **earned-secure** status without ever fully discarding the older substrate. Mary Main's Adult Attachment Interview, hypothetically administered, would yield narrative coherence on most domains but episodic dysfluency around the mother's death and around the first decade of marriage — the subject can name what happened, but the affect attached to it is **either flat or displaced onto present concerns** (Franklin's safety, Johnny's choices). The classic AAI tell — "lack of resolution of loss" — would score positive for Mary Storm and arguably for the miscarried second child.

The behavioral signature is consistent and identifiable across published material: subject **monitors the emotional weather of the room before establishing her own**, calibrates her affect to what the system can tolerate, and pre-positions herself as the stabilizer rather than the destabilizer. This is not personality; this is the residue of being the eight-year-old who had to keep a five-year-old fed while a drunk father broke furniture in the next room.

---

## 6.2 The Master Template — and Its Three Recurrent Casts

The single relational template that subject recapitulates across her life has three roles, and she has cast every significant figure in her adult life into one of them:

- **The Unmoored Brilliant Man**, who must be managed, translated, and forgiven. (Reed Richards is the prototype; Franklin Storm Sr. is the source; even Doom plays this role briefly in the diplomatic frames.)
- **The Reckless Younger Dependent**, who must be parented past his own self-destruction. (Johnny is the prototype; Franklin Jr. inherits some of this; the Future Foundation children collectively occupy a sublimated, healthier version.)
- **The Steady Peer**, the only role in which subject experiences relational rest. (Ben Grimm is the prototype, and his uniqueness in this position is itself diagnostic — subject has **exactly one** peer relationship and has had it for sixty years.)

Every new significant figure entering subject's life is, within weeks, assimilated to one of these three roles. The Namor entanglements over decades read as the system's only sustained attempt to write a **fourth** role — a man who pursues her as sovereign rather than as utility — and the fact that the system cannot stabilize him into the template (he remains intermittent, alien, never integrated) is part of what makes him recurrently dangerous to her marriage.

---

## 6.3 Bonding: How Subject Enters a Relationship

Subject bonds **slowly on the surface, instantly underneath**. The conscious presentation is warm, gracious, measured — the diplomat's opening. Underneath, a rapid triage occurs: the new figure is sorted into the template, threat-assessed for impulsivity and substance-cued unreliability (the paternal screen, always running), and assigned a maintenance load. Within a single interaction she has typically established (a) what this person needs from her, (b) what they are likely to cost her, and (c) what register of self-presentation will keep them functional. The presentation she settles on is then **remarkably stable**; subject does not re-baseline relationships casually.

The bonding tells, longitudinally observable:

- **Use of name.** Subject moves to first-name address quickly with subordinates and children, slowly with peers, and uses Reed's name in three distinct registers — "Reed" (operational), "Reed" (intimate, lower register, often when they are alone in a doorway), and the full "Reed Richards" deployed only when she is publicly correcting him or privately furious. The shift between these is one of the most reliable affect indicators in the file.
- **Physical orientation.** She positions herself at the speaker's three-quarter angle, not face-on, which permits her to monitor the broader room. With Franklin and Valeria she breaks this rule and faces them directly — one of very few signatures of unguarded presence.
- **Initiation of physical contact.** Subject initiates light contact (hand on forearm, palm at the small of the back) as a regulatory gesture toward distressed others; she **rarely** initiates contact for her own comfort. The asymmetry has been stable across all eras.
- **Disclosure cadence.** She discloses one beat behind what the other person has offered, never ahead. This is the parentified child's social grammar — never be more exposed than the person you are managing.

---

## 6.4 Distrust: The Threat-Detection System

Subject's distrust is **slow to declare itself and difficult to reverse once declared**. She does not perform distrust the way Reed performs analytic skepticism or Ben performs working-class wariness; she absorbs anomalies silently, files them, and re-presents them weeks or months later as fully argued conclusions. The pattern is consistent across the Latverian dealings, the post-Civil War assessment of Tony Stark, the early read on the Hate-Monger's influence inside her own household, and the long arc of her relationship to S.H.I.E.L.D. as an institution.

Her trip-wires, ordered by sensitivity:

1. **Substance-cued unreliability or compulsivity.** This is the deepest and earliest wire. Anyone whose behavior pattern-matches to her father's pre-collapse phase triggers a low-level, durable wariness she rarely names. Johnny lives under this surveillance permanently and benignly; the Yancy Street period of Ben's drinking, when written, triggered the same pattern.
2. **Treating people as variables.** When Reed crosses this line, her response is not anger but a specific quality of **silence followed by withdrawal of presence** that is more punishing than any verbalization. She used it during the Negative Zone prison disclosure. She uses it in miniature, weekly.
3. **Condescension that recapitulates the early-marriage register.** This is the wound most visible in micro-behavior. Subject's face does a specific thing — a half-second downward glance, a small tightening at the jaw, return to neutral — that has been drawn consistently by attentive artists since the Byrne era. She does not always answer the condescension; she **always logs it**.
4. **Unilateral action affecting her children.** Trust loss here is structural and slow to repair. Agatha Harkness retained her trust because the relationship was negotiated; Reed lost much of it when he shut down Franklin's mind without consultation, and the trust returned only in increments measurable in years.

What subject does **not** treat as a primary trust violation, and this is diagnostic: **infidelity threat from herself**. The Namor episodes are tolerated by her own self-judgment because she frames them as leverage — as the only tool available to extract response from Reed. Whether this framing is accurate or post-hoc rationalization is a question subject has never permitted herself to fully open.

---

## 6.5 Betrayal: How Subject Is Wounded, and How She Wounds

The betrayals she has sustained are predominantly **betrayals of inclusion** — being moved through the world as someone who will follow rather than someone who must be consulted. The Lee/Kirby decade is one long accumulation of these micro-betrayals; the Byrne era is the eruption of the accumulated weight. The Malice possession is best read as the **somatic ledger of unacknowledged betrayal demanding payment**, externalized as a villain because the family system could not metabolize it as legitimate spousal grievance.

Reed's specific betrayals form a discernible class:
- Decisions affecting her body without her consent (early-pregnancy management, certain medical interventions she only learned about retroactively).
- Decisions affecting Franklin without consultation (the lobotomy, certain Future Foundation curriculum choices).
- Disappearances framed as necessary — the Hickman-era apparent death, the various dimensional vanishings, the Council of Reeds disclosures.
- The Civil War collaboration with the Negative Zone prison and the cloned Thor incident.

The pattern: subject can absorb Reed's **abstraction** (his being elsewhere mentally) almost infinitely; she cannot absorb Reed's **autonomy over her or hers**. The distinction is precise. He can ignore her at dinner; he cannot make decisions about Franklin without her.

When subject herself betrays, the form is consistent: **withdrawal of presence, declared late and decisively**. She does not engage in slow drift, plausible-deniability cooling, or chronic infidelity. The Civil War departure was characteristic — once the threshold was crossed, the separation was announced, executed, and structured. The earlier separation after the Franklin lobotomy followed the same pattern. Subject's betrayals are **legible, justified, and reversible upon repair**. This is the rarest thing about her relational style and the clearest mark of the earned-secure overlay.

The Namor entanglements are the exception — the one zone where subject permits ambiguity rather than declaration. The ambiguity is itself the message to Reed: *I can be unreadable too*.

---

## 6.6 Repair: The Repair Sequence

Subject's repair behavior is the most refined element of her relational toolkit and has been visibly trained on Reed across decades of provocation. The sequence:

1. **Cooling interval.** Subject requires physical or operational distance before repair can begin. The interval scales with the size of the rupture — minutes for daily friction, days for the Negative Zone disclosure, an entire arc for the Franklin lobotomy.
2. **Reframing offer.** Subject is the one who initiates conversation about the rupture, and she does it by **naming the structural issue rather than the affect**. ("This is about you not telling me" — not "I am hurt.") The affective layer is acknowledged in passing rather than centered. This is suppression in service of repair — and it is also the residue of a household where naming feelings did not produce safety.
3. **Demand for concrete behavioral change.** Subject does not accept apology as currency. She accepts changed behavior over time. Reed has learned this; he no longer apologizes verbally without a procedural offer attached.
4. **Calibrated re-entry.** Resumption of intimacy is incremental and asymmetrically initiated by her on her timeline. Reed's attempts to accelerate are received coolly.
5. **Permanent file entry.** Subject does not forgive in the sense of forgetting. The repaired material is integrated into the relationship's working model and will be referenced — sometimes years later — as precedent. This is one of her few unequivocally hard-edged traits.

With Johnny the sequence is shorter and warmer; with Ben it almost never needs to run; with her children it is collapsed to seconds and conducted physically rather than verbally.

---

## 6.7 Intimacy: The Texture of Closeness

Subject experiences intimacy in **at least four distinct registers**, and confuses them less than most people. They are:

- **Maternal intimacy** — unguarded, somatically engaged (she touches her children freely, sleeps near them under threat, sits closer than necessary), and the only register in which her affect runs ahead of her cognition rather than behind it. This is the register in which she is **least covertly powerful**, because she is not managing anyone.
- **Spousal intimacy with Reed** — characterized by a long-running negotiation between physical closeness and cognitive distance. She has learned that Reed expresses love primarily through proximity-to-work (bringing her into his lab, narrating his thinking) rather than through directed emotional attention, and she has accepted this with a substantial private cost. Sexual intimacy, where canonically implied, reads as a domain in which Reed becomes briefly fully present and she briefly stops managing; it is partly **the only place she is permitted to be off-duty**, and this has weighted it disproportionately in the marriage's economy.
- **Sibling intimacy with Johnny** — physical affection used as the channel where words would either embarrass him or escalate him; she ruffles his hair, palms his shoulder, intervenes between him and the consequences of his impulses. The intimacy is dense but asymmetric — she knows him completely, and he knows the version of her that protects him.
- **Peer intimacy with Ben** — characterized by extended companionable silence, the absence of management, dry humor in a register she uses with no one else, and a degree of physical relaxation in his presence that is otherwise absent from her file. Ben is the only adult in her life in whose company she does not appear to be working.

The absence of a **fifth register** — intimate friendship with another adult woman peer of equivalent stature — is one of the more striking gaps in the longitudinal file. Relationships with Alicia Masters, Crystal, Medusa, and Jennifer Walters approach but do not sustain this register. Subject's life has been arranged such that adult women appear primarily as **fellow caregivers, junior charges, or diplomatic counterparts**. She has no Watsonian best friend. This is a clinically meaningful absence and is consistent with the parentified profile: the parentified child is, by structure, isolated from peers because she is doing adult work and peers are not.

---

## 6.8 Dependency: The Direction and Asymmetry of Need

Subject's dependency patterns are **inverted from the early-canon presentation**. The Lee/Kirby surface — subject as the one who needs rescue — was always inaccurate to the underlying flows of the household. The actual dependency vector across sixty years runs **toward her, not from her**: Reed depends on her for the human-systems integration his cognition cannot supply, Johnny depends on her for the structural continuity his impulse-driven life cannot supply, Franklin depends on her for the mortal-frame anchoring his cosmic capacities threaten, and Ben — uniquely — does not depend on her for anything, which is part of why she can rest in his presence.

Subject's own dependencies are **few, narrow, and largely unacknowledged**:

- She depends on Reed for the cognitive sparring that confirms her own intellectual status, even when she is angry at him.
- She depends on the family unit as a holding environment without which her own affect regulation would be measurably more difficult.
- She depends on her power — and this is rarely named — as a **somatic discharge route** for affect that has nowhere else to go. The fields are not only weapons; they are a metabolic system.
- She depends on the role itself. Take away the parentified function and the question of what subject would be becomes acute, and she has historically organized her life to avoid asking it. The most psychologically dangerous gift one could give her would be a year of complete relief.

She does **not** depend on external validation in the conventional sense, on substances, on novelty, on conflict, or on the approval of figures outside her chosen family. This makes her difficult to coerce or seduce; the few successful manipulations of her have all worked by routing through dependent family members rather than through her directly.

---

## 6.9 The Repeated Template, Across Every Significant Relationship

The single relational pattern subject reproduces, with high fidelity and across every era:

**She enters as the apparent junior; assesses the other's unmet needs; takes up the management of those needs without contract; absorbs the cost in silence for an extended period; reaches an internal threshold visible only to her; declares the limit clearly and once; if the other adjusts, the relationship deepens into a permanent obligation she will discharge for life; if the other does not adjust, she withdraws with a finality that surprises the other party because they did not notice the accumulation.**

Cast list:

- **Franklin Storm (father).** Original site of the template. She managed him as a child, absorbed his collapse, reclaimed the relationship in his late-life redemption arc, forgave him on her own terms, mourned him cleanly when he died — which is, in the file, almost the only grief she has been observed to fully complete. The completed mourning of the father is the single most therapeutically significant event in the longitudinal record.
- **Reed Richards.** The template applied at maximum duration and intensity. Sixty years of management, with the limit declared four or five times across the run, each declaration producing structural adjustment. The relationship is now genuinely more equal than it began — not because the original imbalance was illusory but because subject systematically renegotiated it across decades.
- **Johnny Storm.** The template applied as sibling-as-child. The limit has been declared incrementally rather than at a single threshold; Johnny is the one figure with whom subject's standard "declare and withdraw" sequence does not fully execute, because she will not actually withdraw from him. He knows this; she knows he knows; it is the load-bearing dysfunction of the relationship.
- **Ben Grimm.** The template **does not apply**, which is itself the point. Ben presented as needing nothing she could provide that he could not provide himself, and subject's relational system has therefore been able to relate to him as a peer for sixty years without strain. He is the control case proving that her caregiving pattern is responsive to need, not compulsive.
- **Franklin Richards (son).** The template inverted into healthy parenthood, complicated by the cosmic stakes. She manages him with the parentified child's competence and the mother's love; the two run on top of each other and have occasionally conflicted (the years after Reed's lobotomy intervention, when she was managing her son's mind, her husband's guilt, and her own fury simultaneously).
- **Valeria Richards (daughter).** The template inverted again, but with one crucial difference: Valeria is cognitively closer to Reed than to subject, and subject has had to learn to mother a child who reads her the way Reed reads her. The relationship is the cleanest available evidence of subject's growth — she has not allowed Valeria's brilliance to reinstate the early-marriage diminishment.
- **Namor.** The template's structural exception. He pursues her as sovereign, refuses her caregiving, and offers a relational geometry the rest of her life does not provide. Her response is to permit the destabilization in controlled doses. He functions in her psychic economy as **proof of the road not taken**, kept warm enough to remain a live option but never activated.
- **Doctor Doom.** Diplomatic counterpart, occasional rescuer of her child, intermittent enemy. Subject relates to him through a register of cold formality that conceals a more nuanced read — she understands the Reed/Doom mirror better than either man does, and she has on several occasions used that understanding to broker outcomes neither man could have reached alone. The relationship is the clearest example of her **planetary-scale diplomatic application of the parentified skill set**.
- **The Future Foundation children.** The template at its healthiest and most sublimated. Generativity in the Eriksonian sense, with the difference that these children's needs are bounded, scheduled, pedagogical — she gets to give care without it eating her, and the relationship has therapeutic value to her that she does not name.
- **Agatha Harkness.** A rare instance of subject accepting care from another adult woman. Agatha's competence with Franklin permitted subject to **delegate without anxiety**, an act virtually unique in her file. The relationship's eventual disruption was therefore disproportionately painful.

---

## 6.10 Synthesis

Subject's attachment system is the **single most disciplined element of an unusually disciplined psyche**, and it is disciplined precisely because it was forged under conditions that should have broken it. The pattern is legible, repetitive, and — critically — **gradually self-correcting across the longitudinal record**. The early decades show the template running unchecked; the middle decades show subject becoming conscious of it; the late decades show subject choosing when to enact it and when to refuse. She has not escaped the template; she has become its operator.

The relational geometry she has built around herself is, by adult-attachment standards, **anomalously stable for someone with her trauma load**, and the anomaly is held in place by three structures: the marriage (chronically frictional but never severed beyond repair), the team-as-family (the Eriksonian holding environment), and the children (the proof of generativity that keeps despair at bay). Removal of any one of the three would precipitate the kind of crisis she has not had to face since the Byrne era, and the file's primary recommendation, were this dossier predictive rather than retrospective, would be **vigilance during any period in which two of the three are simultaneously destabilized**. That is the configuration in which the parentified child inside the integrated adult would surface, and the question of what subject is *for*, separated from whom she is for, would become operative.

She has not had to answer that question yet. Her life has been arranged — partly by accident, partly by her own quiet design — such that she has not had to. Whether she could is, in this file's assessment, the single most important unanswered question about her.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU INTELLIGENCE DOSSIER — SUSAN STORM RICHARDS
## Section 7: Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms
### Subsection: The Full Defensive Architecture

---

## Preface: How to Read This Subject's Defense Stack

Subject's defensive architecture is unusually **legible** for someone of her trauma load, because two of her primary mechanisms — invisibility and force projection — are externalized into observable physics. A clinician would have to infer most patients' suppression, withdrawal, and boundary-setting from speech, gait, micro-expression, and absence. With this subject, the suppression literally renders her optically absent; the boundary is a measurable photonic shell; the rage produces a visible construct in three-dimensional space. **Her unconscious has a public API.** This makes the file both easier to write and easier to underestimate: an observer who reads only the physical manifestation will miss that the same operations are running, more covertly, at the relational and verbal levels every waking hour.

Defenses are ranked below from most mature (top) to most primitive (bottom), per the Vaillant hierarchy, with behavioral instantiations and longitudinal evidence for each.

---

## I. MATURE DEFENSES (Dominant Register, post-1985)

### 1. Sublimation — *the central organizing defense*

The defense that defines her adult presentation. **Rage at a lifetime of being overridden is converted, in real time, into precisely calibrated force-field work.** This is not metaphor; the somatic-affective coupling is established (force-field amplitude scales with limbic arousal). The Byrne-era expansion of her power suite is, read clinically, the moment subject's unconscious found a discharge route adequate to the accumulated charge. Before 1981, the charge had nowhere to go and produced symptom (the Malice substrate forming silently); after, the charge has a vocation.

Behavioral signatures:
- The flat, almost bored affect she presents while applying enormous force in combat. Civilians and rookies expect strain; she shows none. The affect is bored because the affect is **discharged**.
- The tendency to do her hardest work — sealing rifts, holding domes over cities, pinching a hostile cardiovascular system shut — while continuing a conversation in normal cadence. The work is the regulation.
- A noticeable post-combat composure that her teammates lack. Ben needs to hit something; Johnny needs to fly it off; Reed needs to retreat to a screen. She is already regulated when she lands, because the fight was the regulation.
