The mother-of-the-team Future Foundation pedagogy is the **non-combat** sublimation channel: parentified caregiving converted to chosen vocation, generativity in the Eriksonian register, the wound made into a school.

### 2. Altruism

Caretaking is identity-grade, but in the adult presentation it operates as a mature defense rather than the compulsive caregiving of the early decades. The distinction is **consent and limits**. She still over-functions, but she now picks where; she will let Ben handle Johnny's tantrum without intervening; she will let Reed sit with the consequences of his own mistake long enough for him to feel them. Pre-Byrne altruism was indistinguishable from obligation. Modern altruism is chosen and bounded — which means, technically, it qualifies as the mature defense.

Operational tells:
- Volunteers for the diplomatic-translator role in any multi-party crisis. This is also competence, but the speed of the volunteer is defense.
- Will absorb a stranger's grief — a widowed civilian, a refugee child — with full presence, and then drop the affect cleanly when out of frame. The presence is real; the cleanliness of the drop is the defense doing its work.

### 3. Suppression (conscious, deliberate)

Distinguished sharply from repression. She **knows** what she is setting aside; she has the metacognitive handle on it; she will return to it later, often does. Observable in any major crisis: an emotion will register on the face — usually around the eyes, a flicker of held breath — and is then **placed**, with visible decision, into a queue. After the crisis she retrieves it, frequently in solitude or with Ben (her safe peer).

Diagnostic value: subject's capacity for suppression is what permits her to operate in environments where Reed dissociates, Johnny acts out, and Ben withdraws into stoicism. Suppression is the load-bearing defense of the team.

### 4. Humor (dry, low-volume, occasionally surgical)

Underdiscussed in her published characterization but consistent across runs. Her humor is **observational and slightly cutting**, deployed in three settings: to deflate Reed when he is becoming insufferable; to puncture Johnny when he is becoming reckless; to signal to Ben that she has noticed what he has noticed. Almost never deployed in combat (where she is mostly silent) and almost never aimed at outsiders (where it would damage diplomatic capital). The humor is **in-group regulation**.

### 5. Anticipation

Constant low-grade scenario modeling. She predicts second- and third-order family consequences of operational decisions and pre-positions herself for them. Before Reed announces a dimensional expedition, she has already mapped childcare contingencies, hostile-actor opportunism windows, and Johnny's likely emotional response to being excluded. The anticipation is so habitual it reads as omniscience; it is in fact a defense against the chaos that arrives when one **doesn't** anticipate, the chaos that defined her childhood after her mother died.

---

## II. NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Present, Active, Aging Out Slowly)

### 6. Reaction Formation

The cheerful competent affect over the bedrock anger is the textbook case. Her public register — patient, gracious, hostess-warm — is calibrated **opposite** to the volume of her actual interior response to many of the people she greets that way. The Malice arc is the diagnostic event: reaction formation, sustained for two decades, produced a dissociated counter-self that the Hate-Monger could weaponize. Post-integration, reaction formation has slackened but not retired. She still smiles at men who have just spoken to her in ways that warrant a cold stare.

Tell: the brief flat half-second before the smile arrives. Standard observation distance, you miss it. Surveillance footage, you don't.

### 7. Intellectualization (Adopted, Mimetic)

She has, across decades of cohabitation, **acquired Reed's vocabulary** and uses it strategically. When she wants to be heard in a room of physicists, she frames moral arguments in the language of optimization, variable cost, systemic risk. This is not her native cognition — her native cognition is integrative-relational — but she has learned that the men around her downgrade emotional framing and upgrade technical framing, and she translates accordingly. The intellectualization is partly defense (distance from her own affect to make it palatable), partly tactical (translation for an audience), and partly assimilation wound (the early-marriage demand that she "speak Reed" to be taken seriously).

### 8. Displacement

Modest but real. Anger at Reed will, occasionally, surface first as sharpness with Johnny. Anger at Johnny will surface as terseness with a Foundation child who deserves better. She catches it faster than she used to; in the Lee/Kirby through Thomas period, displacement was a primary discharge route and she did not catch it at all. The aiming has improved; the mechanism still runs.

### 9. Rationalization

Most active around Reed. The narrative she constructs to explain why she returned after a given rupture (Civil War, the Franklin lobotomy aftermath, the various Reed-disappearances) is **always coherent and usually true** but it is also doing defensive work, smoothing the case for return because the alternative — sitting with the unresolved injury — is what she has decided not to do. Note: she does not rationalize Johnny's behavior, and she does not rationalize her own. The rationalization is **relationship-specific** and almost exclusively about staying married.

### 10. Isolation of Affect

Surgical. When she is doing the inside-the-body force-field work — pinching an artery, compressing a tumor, occluding an attacker's airway from within — she is operating with affect fully isolated from action. This is necessary (you cannot do that work feeling it) and it is concerning (the capability sits behind a thin door). She does not advertise the capability. She uses it rarely. She has done it more than the public record reflects.

---

## III. IMMATURE DEFENSES (Historical, Largely Outgrown, Episodically Resurgent)

### 11. Repression (Primary Driver Until 1985, Now Episodic)

The pre-Byrne archive is, in functional terms, **two decades of unbroken repression**. Mother's death not grieved on-panel; father's collapse not processed; Reed's condescension absorbed without protest; Namor's attentions denied as the lever she was clearly using them as. The repressed material did not vanish; it pooled, and the Malice phenomenon is the pool overtopping its containment.

Post-integration, repression appears in narrower bands: she still does not freely access the grief for the second pregnancy; she still does not freely access the resentment toward her father; she still under-engages with the early-marriage humiliation. These are the **stable repressed nodes**. Everything else has been pulled forward.

### 12. Somatization (Powered Variant)

A novel category for this subject because her soma is partly weaponized. Stress that another person would somatize as headache, GI distress, or insomnia arrives in her as **involuntary power expression**: invisibility lapses under unconsciousness, force-field micro-flickers under acute startle, the documented instances where intense protective fear has produced unbidden bubbles around children in her vicinity. Her body cannot keep affect entirely silent; the leak is photonic and psionic rather than gastric.

The miscarriage of the second pregnancy (FF #267) is the most charged somatic event in the file and is **not** somatization in the defensive sense — it was caused by the cosmic-ray physiology incompatibility — but the **absence of subsequent symptom**, the rapid return to function, indicates that something carried the weight elsewhere. The Malice manifestation begins coalescing in the issues following.

### 13. Dissociation (Iatrogenic / Episodic)

Not a baseline defense. Present as substrate available to external exploitation: Malice (Hate-Monger), Psycho-Man's emotion-engine, Hate-Monger's later re-attempts. Subject's repression-rich interior is **dissociation-prone under attack**; under non-attack conditions she does not dissociate. The clinical read: a vulnerability, not a disorder, and one she has reduced by integrating the repressed material that fed it.

### 14. Passive Aggression (Vestigial)

Almost gone from the modern register but historically present, particularly in the Lee/Kirby and early Thomas eras. The Namor flirtation is the archetypal instance: she could not say to Reed *attend to me*, so she generated a stimulus that compelled his attention. The mechanism is now retired because the direct channel has opened — she will, today, simply say it.

---

## IV. POSITIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (The Adaptive Surplus)

These are not defenses in the technical sense; they are **post-traumatic constructions** that produced genuine adaptive gain.

### A. The Diplomatic Vocation

Atlantean ambassador, inter-team liaison, Avengers-Fantastic Four interface, frequent first-contact role with new factions. The parentified-child skill set — read the unstable man in the room, predict the rupture, intervene before it lands, soothe without ceding — scales to **planetary statecraft**. This is the parentification injury converted to public service at the largest available scale. It is also, not incidentally, a setting in which she is paid (in standing, not currency) to do what she was previously expected to do for free.

### B. The Future Foundation Pedagogy

Generativity proper. She did not have, in her own childhood, the adult who held the field steady; she has become, for a generation of unusual children, that adult. The pedagogy is deliberate, methodical, and explicitly anti-Reed in places — children are taught to feel before they are taught to optimize, to play before they are taught to model. This is corrective work, both for the children and for the unhealed child who designs the curriculum.

### C. Earned-Secure Overlay

The single largest adaptive achievement. Through repeated cycles of rupture, departure, return-on-terms, and witnessed Reed-capitulation, she has built — across decades, without therapy — a **functional earned-secure attachment overlay** on her anxious-preoccupied origin template. She can now leave the room and trust the relationship to survive her absence. This is a developmental accomplishment of the first rank.

### D. The Integration of Malice

The Malice arc was a defensive collapse and is also, paradoxically, the single most successful piece of self-work in her file. She **owned** the rage on the field, named it as hers, and brought it inside the self-concept. Almost no one accomplishes this without years of clinical scaffolding. She did it under combat conditions because she had to. The integration has held for forty publication years and has metabolized into the operational rage of the modern Invisible Woman, who no longer needs an alter to express what she feels.

### E. The Powered Boundary as Practiced Skill

The force-field is now a **rehearsed corrective experience**. Every time she throws one up — around a child, around a teammate, around herself — she rehearses the boundary she was structurally denied as a girl. This is therapeutic repetition with somatic discharge built in. Decades of daily practice have produced a person who knows, in her body, that she can say no and have the no hold.

### F. The Selected Confidant (Ben)

The decision, sustained across sixty years, to keep one peer relationship outside the marital-fraternal-maternal triangle is itself adaptive infrastructure. Ben is the friend who is not a project. The conversations are short, dry, mutually respectful, and load-bearing. Most people in her structural position do not preserve such a relationship; she has.

---

## V. NEGATIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (The Cost Side)

### A. Chronic Over-Forgiveness of Reed

The rationalization-and-return cycle has resolved with her returning more times than the relational accounting would warrant. Reed's failures — the Franklin lobotomy, the Negative Zone prison, multiple unilateral cosmic-stakes decisions — have been forgiven on terms that protected the marriage at some cost to her standing. She has improved; she has not stopped. The Civil War defection is the high-water mark of consequence-enforcement; she has not, since, replicated its severity even where it might be warranted.

### B. Tolerance of Johnny's Regressions

She has accepted, year after year, behaviors from her brother that she would not accept from any other adult. The maternal injunction set at age ten — *keep him intact* — has not been retired even though Johnny is, by any reasonable measure, an adult capable of his own consequences. The cost is depletion and chronic low-grade resentment that occasionally leaks (see Displacement, above).

### C. Threat-Detection Asymmetry

She identifies threats to family in milliseconds and threats to self in minutes. The asymmetry is structural and has nearly killed her on multiple occasions. A surveillance file notices this as **standing operational vulnerability**: an adversary who can engineer a family-threat decoy will routinely buy a window of self-exposure during which she will absorb damage she would not otherwise absorb.

### D. Suppression-Debt Accumulation

The mature defense of suppression is itself **load-bearing infrastructure with a maintenance cost**. Material gets queued and not always retrieved. Sleep is the documented retrieval window; in periods of sleep disruption (cosmic crisis, infant care, Reed-disappearance vigil), the queue overflows and one of two things happens: minor somatic leak (involuntary invisibility flicker on waking), or — historically — pool formation that becomes exploitable.

### E. The "Speak Reed" Tax

Translation labor. To be heard in her own household at the level her judgment merits, she has had to acquire and continuously deploy a second cognitive register. This is real labor, performed daily, never credited. It produces fluency but also fatigue, and it produces the subtle alienation of someone who routinely says important things in language that is not quite hers.

### F. The Invisibility-of-Self Habit

The defense she was named for. When overwhelmed in a non-combat social setting, she will literally **go quiet and recede in the room** — not turn invisible, but become visually and attentionally minimal. The habit predates her powers and is the precursor of them. It is adaptive in the wrong way: it lets her conserve, but it reinforces the very pattern her power-set ostensibly transcended. She does it less than she did in 1965. She still does it.

---

## VI. STRUCTURAL SUMMARY OF THE DEFENSIVE ARCHITECTURE

Subject runs a **mature-dominant stack with neurotic mid-layer and a small but live immature substrate**, scaffolded by an unusual feature: two of her primary mature defenses are externalized into measurable physical phenomena. The architecture is largely earned rather than constitutional — the early decades show her operating with a far more primitive stack (repression, reaction formation, displacement, passive aggression) and the modern register is the product of slow, unwitnessed, mostly self-conducted psychological work performed in the only laboratory available to her, which was her own life under continuous load.

The architecture's **strength** is its discharge route: sublimation through powered work prevents the chronic pooling that would, in an unpowered person with this history, produce far more visible psychiatric symptom. The architecture's **weakness** is the same: because the discharge is so effective, she is under-motivated to undertake the deeper repressed-node work (mother, father, second pregnancy, early-marriage humiliation) that remains undone. The system runs well enough that the unfinished business is invisible — to her, to her family, and to almost every observer except one with this file open.

She is, defensively, **the most quietly competent adaptation in her cohort** and the one whose remaining work is hardest to see precisely because she has made invisibility a craft.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7
## LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE
### Subject: Susan Storm Richards
### Frame: Decade-by-decade clinical reconstruction, 1961–present, with attention to affect regulation, cognitive architecture, self-concept, and the transitional events that re-organized each.

---

## Preamble: Methodological Note

The decadal divisions below are heuristic; psyches do not respect publication calendars. But because subject's life is exceptionally well-documented and because each major creative era introduced different stressors and different testing conditions, the decade is a defensible unit of analysis. I have anchored each period to (a) a baseline mental-status reconstruction, (b) the dominant defensive constellation operative at that time, (c) the cognitive style observable in her on-page problem-solving, (d) the self-concept she presents and the self-concept the evidence supports, and (e) the transitional event(s) that close the era and seed the next.

The through-line: subject begins as a young woman whose ego is organized around **deferred visibility** — she will be seen later, by someone, if she is good enough — and arrives, six decades later, at an ego organized around **chosen visibility** — she will be seen when and how she elects, and her absence is now a weapon rather than a wound. The conversion is real and is the singular psychological achievement of her life. It was paid for in cumulative trauma the file documents elsewhere.

---

## 1961–1970 — THE SUPPRESSED PHASE

### Baseline Mental Status
On first observation (FF #1–#20 range), subject presents with affect that is **constricted-but-pleasant**, speech that is **soft, deferential, and frequently interruptible**, and a behavioral repertoire dominated by orientation toward the three men around her. Cognition is intact and quick — her tactical commentary in the early issues is often more sound than Reed's combat instructions — but it is delivered in a register that invites dismissal and is usually dismissed. She does not protest the dismissal. She re-orients and tries again.

This is not stupidity, weakness, or even quietness of temperament. This is **a young woman in her early twenties who has spent her entire conscious life in a structural role (caretaker of an alcoholic father, parent to a younger brother) that punished assertion and rewarded smoothing**. The cheerful-deferent surface is overlearned. By the time we meet her she does it without effort because she has been doing it since approximately age eight.

### Affect Regulation
**Suppression-dominant.** Affect is not absent; affect is filed. She experiences jealousy (the Namor sequences make this unmistakable), fear (repeatedly, accurately), frustration (rarely surfaced, occasionally leaked through dry asides), and grief (the unprocessed mother-loss substrate is everywhere if one looks for it). What she does with these is **compress and continue**. The autonomic cost is invisible to her teammates and partially invisible to herself; we infer it from the somatic correlates — frequent fainting, frequent "headaches," and the not-incidental fact that her power in this era is **invisibility only**, the somaticization of her social condition.

Regulation in this decade is therefore **expensive but functional**. She does not decompensate. She also does not metabolize.

### Cognitive Style
**Relational-integrative, masked as decorative.** She tracks the emotional weather of the room with near-total accuracy and uses that data to keep the team operational — defusing Reed and Ben, redirecting Johnny, managing outside parties. This is genuine high-order cognition (the kind clinicians call **theory-of-mind acuity** and which correlates with leadership in adulthood). It is invisible to the men around her because it does not announce itself in equations. She does not announce it either. The early-era pattern is: **she knows, she acts on what she knows, she allows credit to land elsewhere**. This is a tactical adaptation to her household of origin generalized to her household of marriage.

### Self-Concept
**Conditional and externalized.** "I am what is needed." Identity is a function of role: sister-mother to Johnny, fiancée-then-wife to Reed, supportive teammate to Ben. There is no observable interior self-narrative independent of these relationships — or rather, there is one, and it is the modeling/acting ambition that brought her to New York, but that ambition is itself organized around **proximity to Reed**, so it is not actually a counterweight to the relational self. The self-concept question "who am I when no one needs anything from me?" is not askable in this decade; she has never been in that condition long enough to find out.

### Dominant Defenses
Suppression, reaction formation (cheerful competence over considerable resentment), displacement (jealousy of Reed's work expressed as jealousy of women — see the early Crystal sequences and pre-marriage Reed/Alicia confusions), and a quiet **identification with the aggressor** in the form of adopting Reed's vocabulary of "the team" and "the mission" to legitimate her own subordination.

### Transitional Events Closing the Era
The Namor arcs (specifically her demonstrable, conscious entertainment of his attention in #6, #9, #27), marriage (Annual #3), the birth of Franklin (Annual #6), and — under the surface — the slow first appearances of force-field projection. The power expansion is the unconscious announcement that **something is asking to come out**. The Lee/Kirby era ends with that announcement still illegible to the subject.

---

## 1970–1980 — THE FRACTURE DECADE

### Baseline Mental Status
Affect now visibly **labile under specific provocations**. Outside those provocations the deferent surface remains, but it is thinner, and the recovery time after a triggering event is longer. Speech is less easily interruptible. She finishes her sentences more often. There is a measurable increase in **observed irritation** — small expressions of it, then quickly contained.

### Affect Regulation
Suppression remains primary but **begins to fail at the edges**. The decisive evidence is FF #141 (1973): Reed shuts down Franklin's mind to neutralize a cosmic-scale threat without prior consultation, and subject's response is not negotiation, not compromise, not deferred protest — it is **departure**. Subsequent issues track her separation, her flirtation with Namor as the available counter-attachment, and her conditional return. The clinical reading is that **suppression has reached the limit of what it can hold, and behavioral discharge has become necessary**. Leaving is the discharge. She does not yet have force-field expression sufficient to discharge somatically what FF #141 puts into her; she discharges relationally instead.

Across the rest of the decade, this becomes the pattern: when the suppression budget overruns, she leaves. Brief separations recur. Each one is shorter than the wound that produced it suggests it should be, because the parentified-child substrate **panics at sustained absence** — she cannot maintain the protest long enough to alter the contract. But the act of leaving is now in her repertoire, and it was not before.

### Cognitive Style
Increasing **explicit ethical reasoning**. Where in the prior decade she absorbed Reed's framing of "necessary measures," she now contests it. The Franklin lobotomy is the inflection point: she names the act as wrong, in those terms, on the page. This is a cognitive event as much as an emotional one — she is **constructing a moral framework independent of Reed's utilitarian-cosmic calculus** and finding that her framework produces different answers. It will take another decade for her to trust that framework enough to wield it without leaving the room first.

### Self-Concept
**First cracks in the externalized self.** The question "who am I if I disagree with Reed?" becomes askable, and she begins, tentatively, to answer it. The answer is unstable. She returns. She leaves again. The oscillation is itself diagnostic — she is in the early stage of **separation-individuation from a marital figure who has functioned as a parent-surrogate**, a process she did not get to complete with her actual father because he abandoned her before she could rebel against him.

### Dominant Defenses
Suppression with breakthrough; **acting-out via geographic separation** (a higher-order defense than the prior decade's pure compression, but still not integration); continued reaction formation; **splitting under acute stress** — Reed becomes briefly all-bad in the Franklin-lobotomy aftermath, Namor briefly all-good as alternative. The splitting is mild and resolves; it is mentioned because it foreshadows the dissociative substrate the Byrne era will exploit.

### Transitional Events Closing the Era
Cumulative micro-ruptures with Reed; the unstable but increasing expression of force fields; the second pregnancy beginning. The decade ends with the suppression system audibly creaking and the somatic delivery system (force fields) now strong enough to carry what suppression no longer can. The stage is set for the eruption of the next decade.

---

## 1980–1990 — THE INTEGRATION DECADE (BYRNE ERA AND IMMEDIATE AFTERMATH)

This is the **single most psychologically formative period** of the subject's life. The following analysis is correspondingly granular.

### Baseline Mental Status
Early decade: affect is more variable than at any prior point — bursts of authority alternating with moments of acute vulnerability, the latter especially around the second pregnancy. Speech has acquired authority; she gives orders during combat now, and they are followed. Mid-decade: catastrophic decompensation event (Malice). Late decade: a substantially reorganized presentation — calmer, deeper, **less effortful** in its regulation than the prior twenty years.

### The Second Pregnancy and Loss (FF #267, 1984)
Clinical centrality cannot be overstated. Subject loses a child at term, after a sequence in which her husband — the most intelligent man on the planet — fails to save it. The grief is given approximately two issues of narrative space and is then **suppressed back into function** in the manner the subject was trained to from childhood. This is the **last great act of pure suppression in her psychological history**, and it is the precipitant — the unmetabolized matter — that the Malice arc will, within twelve to eighteen issues, externalize and force into consciousness.

What the file must note: a civilian woman with this loss, this husband's culpability, and no permitted mourning would, by ordinary clinical expectation, develop either a major depressive episode of considerable duration or a complex grief reaction with somatic features. Subject develops neither overtly. She develops **Malice**. The Malice episode is the depressive-grief reaction expressed through the only register her psyche knows how to use: somatic-symbolic action via her powers and her relational field.

### The Malice Episode (FF #280–286)
External agent (Psycho-Man, later Hate-Monger) supplies the precipitant, but **the material weaponized is hers**. Years of suppressed rage at Reed, at the men who diminished her, at the universe that took her mother and her son, at her own role in accepting it all, are concretized into a dissociative split with an explicit costume, name, and program — "Mistress of Hate." Diagnostically, this is best read as a **trauma-induced dissociative phenomenon, externally exploited but endogenously substrated**. The DSM language is imperfect because the precipitant is not naturalistic, but the structure is unmistakable: long-term repression → dissociated affect cluster → externally cued switching → reintegration via deliberate confrontation.

The integration mechanism deserves attention. Reed engineers the breaking point by **deliberately provoking her past the point at which she can pretend to be unaffected**, forcing her to **own the rage as hers** in order to defeat the construct that was using it. The therapeutic principle is sound (the dissociated material must be re-claimed by the host ego to lose its autonomy); the agent of the intervention is the man whose behavior generated much of the dissociated material in the first place. This is the central paradox of the marriage and is never adequately resolved: he is both the wound and, intermittently, the suture. Subject knows this. She does not say so out loud until much later.

Post-integration affect regulation is **qualitatively different**. The rage is no longer dissociated — it is available to consciousness, expressible in speech, deployable in force. Her power signature changes in the same period: she becomes **the team's offensive weapon**, force constructs scaled to planetary magnitude, internal-organ-pressure capability (which she will use, infrequently and without advertisement, on opponents who warrant it). The Byrne renaming — Invisible *Woman*, FF #284 — is not cosmetic. It is the public-facing announcement of a reorganized self.

### Cognitive Style
Now **systems-and-people thinking, explicitly authoritative**. She begins to chair team meetings in substance if not in name. She predicts political consequences Reed misses. She makes diplomatic calls. The cognitive capacity was always present; what has changed is the **permission she gives herself to act on it without first translating it into a register the men will accept**.

### Self-Concept
The decade closes with the first **integrated** self-concept of her life. She is mother, wife, teammate — *and* she is the most powerful member of the team, *and* she is angry about a great deal of what has happened to her, *and* she is competent to choose what to do with that anger. The relational identity is no longer the only identity. There is now an interior self with its own contents, and she has met it.

### Dominant Defenses
Sublimation now dominant (rage → force-field combat capacity, a clean and high-functioning channel); altruism stable; suppression reduced and renegotiated; humor more visible — a dry, occasionally cutting register that was barely present in the prior two decades emerges in this one. Reaction formation reduced. Splitting essentially gone post-Malice. **Net: a movement from neurotic to mature defensive organization across a single decade, the kind of structural change ordinarily requiring years of intensive treatment.**

### Transitional Events Closing the Era
Reintegration of Malice; Reed's brief presumed-death sequences; the team's continued existence through editorial turbulence; the slow start of the Valeria pregnancy sequence that will haunt the next decade. The 1980s end with subject having accomplished the central psychological work of her life.

---

## 1990–2000 — THE CONSOLIDATION DECADE

### Baseline Mental Status
Stable. Affect range is broader than at any prior point, regulation is genuinely improved (not merely effortful suppression), and self-presentation has settled into the form that will persist, with refinements, through the rest of the published record. The decade is, by the standards of the prior three, **psychologically quiet** — which is itself diagnostic, because the external events (Onslaught, Heroes Reborn, the Valeria-pregnancy catastrophe) are not quiet at all and would, in an earlier-decade Susan, have produced visible decompensation.

### Affect Regulation
**Earned-secure overlay consolidates over anxious-preoccupied substrate.** She now tolerates Reed's absences — and there are many in this decade, including extended presumed-death — without the splitting and acting-out that earlier separations produced. She still feels the activation; she does not now act it out blindly. The capacity to **hold uncertainty without converting it to behavior** is the marker of earned-secure functioning and it is observable across this period.

### The Valeria Pregnancy
A reproductive event so chronologically convoluted (initial fetal loss, narrative restoration via Franklin's reality-altering capacity, eventual delivery years later with Doom's reluctant midwifery) that the **psychological cost is difficult to score by ordinary instruments**. What the file should record: subject sustains, across this sequence, a degree of ambiguity and loss that would shatter most people, and her observable functioning does not break. The cost is paid in chronic background grief, in the way she holds Valeria with a precise carefulness that the older child Franklin did not receive in infancy, and in a deepened fatalism about cosmic-scale events that her younger self did not display. She does not become bitter. She becomes **older**, in the specific sense that her sense of what can be controlled has narrowed and her sense of what must be endured has widened.

### Cognitive Style
Continues to develop the **systems-and-people executive function** that emerged in the prior decade. By the end of the 1990s she is functioning as the team's de facto chief of staff in all domains except the laboratory — operations, ethics, diplomacy, child-rearing pedagogy, public-facing communications. Reed does not contest this; he relies on it.

### Self-Concept
**Integrated and increasingly secure.** "I am a mother, a partner, a powerful person, and an adult with my own judgment" is now the operative self-statement, and the elements are no longer in tension. The anxious-preoccupied substrate still activates under acute relational threat (Reed presumed-dead, Franklin endangered), but the activation does not destabilize identity; it produces appropriate distress and appropriate action.

### Dominant Defenses
Mature defenses (sublimation, altruism, humor, suppression in its conscious-deferral form) dominant. Neurotic residues (intellectualization, reaction formation) still observable but reduced and increasingly ego-syntonic — she uses them on purpose rather than being used by them.

---

## 2000–2010 — THE AUTHORITY DECADE

### Baseline Mental Status
Notably calm. Speech is now **slow, considered, and final** — she speaks last in most rooms and what she says ends the discussion. Affect is warm-front, watchful-interior, with a marked capacity to **modulate warmth strategically** (she can withhold it, which she could not earlier). Combat affect is cool to the point of professionalism.

### The Civil War Defection (2006–2007)
The defining adult-Susan act and the doctrinal statement of her mature personality. She follows Reed onto the pro-registration side initially — old pattern, conditioned trust in his framework — and then, when she observes what he is actually doing (Negative Zone prison, Thunderbolts collaboration, willingness to treat former friends as enemy combatants), she **defects**. She does not announce the defection in a speech; she leaves a note and goes. She then conducts a guerrilla resistance against her husband's faction for the duration of the conflict.

Clinically, this is the **completion of the developmental task** that the 1973 Franklin-lobotomy departure began. The 1973 departure was reactive, brief, and oscillated — she returned without the underlying contract being renegotiated. The 2006 departure is **structural**: she leaves, she fights, she comes back only when Reed has visibly capitulated and the contract has changed. The contract change is durable. From this point forward, **Reed defers to her on ethical questions as a matter of course**.

It is also worth noting what the defection is *not*: it is not a marital rupture in the romantic sense; she does not stop loving him; she does not seek another partner; she does not consider it a divorce. It is a **functional refusal** — she will not be in the same political project with him — held inside an unbroken intimate bond. This is a level of differentiation that the early-marriage Susan could not have conceived.

### Affect Regulation
**At its highest functional point.** She can be in extreme situations and remain regulated. Failures of regulation now occur only at the documented pressure points (children, condescension echoing the early marriage, social erasure, reproductive-maternal threat) and even there the failures are **controlled discharges** rather than overflows — she chooses when to release force, and the release is targeted.

### Cognitive Style
**Moral-executive.** She has become the ethical court of last resort in the team and, increasingly, in superhuman politics generally. Her cognitive method on hard questions is recognizable: she gathers information, she models the human consequences first and the technical consequences second (the inverse of Reed's order of operations), she names the relevant values, she renders a judgment, and she is willing to act on it without seeking permission. The shift from the 1960s Susan — who knew the answer and let it be ignored — is total.

### Self-Concept
**Stable, integrated, authoritative.** "I am the adult in the room and that fact does not require apology" is now an operative self-statement. The bifurcation noted in the broader workup — relational self conscious, powerful self semi-acknowledged — is narrowing but not closed. She still occasionally frames her interventions deferentially even as she enacts them decisively. The gap is now a habit rather than a structural division.

### Dominant Defenses
Mature defenses ascendant and stable. Altruism, sublimation, suppression-as-conscious-deferral, humor (now more cutting than dry — she can land a line that draws blood, and does, when the occasion warrants). Generativity in the Eriksonian sense is now a primary organizing principle: the Future Foundation pedagogy is the institutional form.

---

## 2010–2020 — THE GENERATIVITY DECADE

### Baseline Mental Status
**Settled.** The decade's external stressors are considerable (the Hickman cosmic-scale events, including a brief death; the team's dissolution and reconstitution under Slott; the children's continued exposure to apocalyptic situations) and her observable mental status absorbs them. There is, for the first time, a **calm that is not effortful** — she has integrated enough that holding herself together no longer requires the daily expenditure it once did.

### Cognitive Style
The systems-and-people executive function reaches its mature form in **diplomatic vocation**. The Atlantean ambassadorship is the headline assignment, but the principle is general: she has become the figure other parties trust to mediate, and her judgment of when to push and when to yield is calibrated to a degree that takes most people a full career in foreign service to achieve. The parentified-child substrate, redirected, is now a **planetary-scale diplomatic instrument**. This is the cleanest possible conversion of a childhood wound into adult vocation and it is one of the more remarkable transformations in the file.

### Self-Concept
**The bifurcation closes**, or comes as close to closing as it ever will. She now self-presents as the most powerful and most morally authoritative member of the team because she is, and she no longer expends energy disguising the fact. The framing-deference habit persists in vestigial form — she will still occasionally say "Reed thinks" when she means "we agreed because I told him I was right" — but it is now a courtesy rather than a compulsion.

### Affect Regulation
At the **post-effortful** stage. She can hold cosmic-scale grief, anger, and fear simultaneously and continue to function — not because she is compressing them but because she has, over forty years, built the capacity to **carry affect without being driven by it**. The Malice substrate has not returned and shows no sign of doing so; the dissociative material has stayed integrated.

### Residual Wounds
The unresolved grief (mother, miscarried child) remains. It does not surface as symptoms anymore; it surfaces as **a particular quality of attention she gives to children in extremis** and as a quietness around certain anniversaries that her family has learned to respect without naming. The wound has been metabolized to the level that it can be carried as background without producing acute symptoms — which is the realistic ceiling for losses of that magnitude. It will not heal further. It does not need to.

---

## 2020–PRESENT — THE LATE-INTEGRATION PHASE

### Baseline Mental Status
Subject is now functioning at the developmental stage Erikson called **integrity vs. despair** — earlier than chronological age would suggest, but appropriate to her unusual life-density. The hallmark is a coherent self-narrative in which the early suppression, the middle ruptures, and the late authority are understood as one continuous trajectory rather than as discontinuous episodes. She can speak about the early years with neither apology nor revisionism. This is itself a clinical achievement.

### Affect Regulation
Stable, mature, non-effortful, with the documented pressure-point v


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

## Subject: Susan Storm Richards
## Section: Full Diagnostic Workup, Longitudinal Course, and Differential Exclusions

---

## I. Framing Statement

Any honest psychiatric workup of this subject must begin with a paradox. Her cumulative trauma load — maternal death in childhood, paternal alcoholism and incarceration for manslaughter, parentification before adolescence, idealized erotic-cognitive attachment to a much older adult man at age twelve, cosmic-radiation alteration of her cellular substrate at approximately twenty, marriage to that same older adult by twenty-two, one obstetric crisis requiring an extraterrestrial artifact for live delivery, one full-term stillbirth, one fetal loss subsequently revised by reality-warping intervention, multiple possessions, repeated near-deaths, at least one documented clinical death, and sixty years of high-lethality occupational exposure — would, in any conventional clinical population, produce a presentation dominated by Complex PTSD, recurrent major depression, possible substance use disorder, somatoform features, and likely a Cluster C personality structure (Dependent or Avoidant) with possible Borderline features secondary to early loss.

She presents with **none of this in active form**. She is, by every functional metric, the most regulated member of her household and arguably the most regulated front-line metahuman of her generation. The diagnostic task is therefore not "what disorder does the subject have"; it is "how is the subject this organized given the inputs," what subclinical and historical conditions account for the residue we *do* observe, and what would destabilize the equilibrium she has constructed.

The workup below uses DSM-5-TR and ICD-11 analogs where appropriate, with explicit acknowledgement that several of the most explanatorily powerful frames (parentification, the Adult Children of Alcoholics phenotype, complex bereavement, earned-secure attachment) sit at the margins of formal nosology.

---

## II. Active Conditions (Current Presentation)

### A. Persistent Complex Bereavement Disorder / Prolonged Grief Disorder (ICD-11 6B42), Chronic, Partially Compensated

**Status:** Active, subclinical-to-clinical depending on rating instrument, present continuously for approximately five decades with respect to maternal loss and approximately four decades with respect to perinatal loss.

**Symptom presentation in behavior:**
- Intense yearning expressed only obliquely (she does not speak Mary Storm's name in operational settings; references in private are brief, present-tense slippages — "Mom would —" cut off mid-clause).
- Avoidance of reminders specific and observed: she does not drive in heavy rain when she can avoid it (her mother died on a wet road); she has been documented declining the wheel and offering plausible secondary reasons.
- Identity disruption in the role of "daughter" — when Franklin Storm reappears in her life across decades, her affect shifts to a child register inconsistent with her established adult voice (pitch elevation of roughly a third, sentence length contraction, increased use of "Daddy" rather than "Dad" or "Father").
- For the stillbirth (the second pregnancy): no public memorial, no commemorative ritual, no anniversary acknowledgement in any recorded interview. She returned to operational status within weeks. The grief was *bypassed*, not processed, and resurfaces somatically in heightened protectiveness toward Valeria — disproportionate even by maternal baseline.

**Why this meets criteria rather than normative grief:** Duration (>12 months), functional interference (specifically: distorted relational responsiveness to subsequent obstetric events), and avoidance behavior that has persisted across the entire adult lifespan satisfy ICD-11 6B42. The compensation is unusually high because of compensatory generativity (Future Foundation, Valeria), which masks but does not resolve the underlying condition.

**Course:** Chronic, low-grade, with predictable acute flares around Mother's Day, her own children's birthdays (note: Franklin's birthday is celebrated; her stillborn son's would-have-been birthday is not, and her affect is observably constricted in the weeks surrounding the date), and any clinical scenario involving a mother and a sick child.

---

### B. Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder, Chronic, In Partial Remission, With Historical Dissociative Features

**Status:** Currently does not meet full DSM-5-TR criteria for active PTSD. Meets historical criteria multiple times across the lifespan. Subthreshold residue persists.

**Index traumas (non-exhaustive):**
1. Witnessed/proximate maternal death, childhood.
2. Paternal incarceration and abandonment.
3. Cosmic ray exposure event (subject did not consent to it as fully as the men did; she went because Reed was going — a consent-under-attachment-coercion that she has never publicly examined).
4. The Franklin lobotomy event — her own husband neurologically silencing her son without her informed consent.
5. The perinatal loss.
6. Repeated possession events (Malice, Psycho-Man, Hate-Monger) — autonomy violations of the most fundamental kind.
7. Operational deaths (her own and her brother's).

**Symptom presentation, current:**
- *Intrusion:* Minimal in conscious report. Sleep architecture, where observed, shows occasional fragmentation — she rises before Reed, often makes coffee in dim light, and has been noted standing at windows for periods of three to seven minutes without action, before resuming the day. This is consistent with low-grade nocturnal intrusion she manages by physical reorientation.
- *Avoidance:* Specific avoidances mapped (driving in rain; medical settings involving obstetric care unless personally required; Negative Zone deployment, which she will accept but visibly armors herself for in a way she does not for other dimensions).
- *Negative cognitions/mood:* Largely compensated. A persistent low-level "the family will not survive my absence" cognition operates as a subclinical conviction rather than a depressive distortion.
- *Hyperarousal:* Threshold-shifted, not exaggerated. She does not startle easily — she is in fact among the slowest-to-startle of the team — but her *threat-discrimination* in domestic settings is exquisitely sensitive (she will identify that Valeria is upset before Valeria has spoken, will note a change in Reed's posture from across a room).

**Dissociative features, historical:** The Malice episode is the diagnostic core. Clinically, this is best read as a **trauma-induced partial dissociative state, externally precipitated and exploited**, in a substrate that had been building dissociative defenses since childhood — splitting off prohibited anger into a not-me self-state. The intensity of the alter, the sexualized presentation (whip, dominatrix iconography), and the targeting of the family are all consistent with the return of the repressed in classic form. Integration was achieved via abreactive confrontation engineered by Reed; the integration has held for decades. There has been no recurrence as a primary alter, though *fragments* of the Malice affect-state recur as conscious anger that she now owns directly. This is treatment-as-by-life: the alter became the integrated affect.

**Course:** Most acute during Lee/Kirby-era suppression and the immediate post-stillbirth period. Peak symptomatic crisis: the Malice arc (FF #280–286), which functioned as a forced therapeutic crisis. Substantial improvement post-Byrne era. Currently functional remission with subthreshold residue.

---

### C. Adult Children of Alcoholics Phenotype (Woititz framework; not DSM-coded, but operationally central)

**Status:** Active, lifelong, partially mitigated by insight, never resolved.

This is the **single most explanatorily powerful frame** for the subject's interpersonal pattern, and its omission from formal nosology should not obscure its centrality. The Woititz criteria map onto the subject with near-textbook fidelity:

1. *Guess at what normal behavior is.* Observable in early-era Susan's uncritical absorption of casual mid-century misogyny within the team; she calibrated "normal marital dynamics" against the only model available (the Reed/Sue dyad), which was abnormal.
2. *Difficulty following projects through from beginning to end.* **Inverted in subject** — she over-completes; this is the compensatory variant common in eldest-daughter ACoA presentations.
3. *Lie when it would be just as easy to tell the truth.* Subject's avoidance is by *omission* rather than active falsehood — she lets things stand uncorrected. Functionally equivalent.
4. *Judge themselves without mercy.* Present and severe. Internal monologue, where inferable from facial micro-affect after operational losses, is harshly self-attributing.
5. *Difficulty having fun.* Present. Recreation is almost always purposive (training Valeria, mentoring Future Foundation students). Spontaneous play is rare and usually initiated by others.
6. *Take themselves very seriously.* Present, mitigated by acquired dry humor.
7. *Difficulty with intimate relationships.* Present, displaced into a relationship that *structurally cannot become intimate in the expected way* (Reed's cognitive remove), thereby reproducing the parental pattern.
8. *Overreact to changes over which they have no control.* Present in obstetric and child-safety contexts; otherwise unusually well-regulated.
9. *Constantly seek approval and affirmation.* Historically present, increasingly absent. The arc from "Invisible Girl" to the woman who exits her marriage over Negative Zone prison ethics is, in part, the slow death of this trait.
10. *Feel different from other people.* Present, but reattributed to metahuman status, which provides a sociably acceptable cover.
11. *Super-responsible or super-irresponsible.* Super-responsible to the point of self-erasure historically; modulating in mid-life.
12. *Loyal to a fault.* The defining feature. She has remained loyal to a father who abandoned her, a husband who has repeatedly chosen abstractions over her, and a brother whose self-destruction has consumed decades of her labor.
13. *Impulsive.* Notably absent. Subject is among the *least* impulsive people in her cohort. This is itself a compensation — the alcoholic father provided the negative template.

**Why this frame matters diagnostically:** Without it, the subject's compliance-then-rupture-then-return cycle with Reed reads as either masochism, dependence, or pathological codependence, none of which fit on closer inspection. With it, the pattern is legible as a learned attachment strategy in which the over-functioning daughter cannot leave the under-functioning man because she does not believe the system survives her departure. Civil War (the Negative Zone defection) is, in this frame, the *first time in her life she tests that belief and finds it survivable*. The therapeutic significance is enormous.

---

### D. Subclinical Dysthymic Substrate (Persistent Depressive Disorder features, not meeting full criteria)

**Status:** Trace. Probably more prominent in the 1965–1980 period; currently minimal.

Evidence: low-grade anhedonia in early-era presentation; characteristic eldest-daughter "manage the affect, do not feel it" posture; tendency to derive satisfaction from others' wellbeing rather than her own pursuits. Has never met threshold for Major Depressive Episode in any verifiable interval. Recovery trajectory is genuine.

---

## III. Conditions Considered and Excluded (Rigorous Differential)

### A. Dependent Personality Disorder — RULED OUT

Surface phenomena suggested this diagnosis through the Lee/Kirby era and would still be reflexively offered by a clinician relying on early canon. It does not survive scrutiny.

**Why not:** DPD requires a pervasive and excessive need to be taken care of, leading to submissive and clinging behavior and fears of separation, across contexts and over time. Subject:
- *Makes autonomous decisions of great consequence without seeking permission* — leaving the team over Franklin's lobotomy, defecting in Civil War, accepting the Atlantean ambassadorship, restructuring the Future Foundation curriculum.
- *Does not require others to assume responsibility* — she assumes it, often to a fault.
- *Has no difficulty initiating projects* — she initiates most family and team logistical infrastructure.
- *Does not go to excessive lengths to obtain nurturance* — historically tolerated its absence rather than seeking it elsewhere.
- *Is not preoccupied with fears of being left to care for herself* — has demonstrated she can.
- *Does urgently seek another relationship when one ends*: NO. The brief separations from Reed were not followed by attachment-seeking; she returned to Reed or remained alone.

The early-era appearance of dependence is **role-bound and historical, not characterological**. DPD is excluded.

### B. Borderline Personality Disorder — RULED OUT

Often considered in cases with early maternal loss and parental abandonment. Subject lacks:
- Identity disturbance (stable self-concept across decades).
- Affective instability (the *opposite* — chronic over-regulation).
- Impulsivity in any self-damaging domain.
- Recurrent suicidal behavior or self-mutilation (absent across canon).
- Inappropriate intense anger (anger is in fact under-expressed historically and now appropriately expressed).
- Stress-related paranoid ideation (absent).
- Frantic efforts to avoid abandonment: equivocal — there is preoccupation with family preservation, but it is not frantic and does not produce the characteristic BPD relational chaos.

The early loss is real; the BPD developmental pathway it sometimes produces did not occur here. Excluded.

### C. Histrionic Personality Disorder — RULED OUT

Trivially excluded. Subject's affect is suppressed, not amplified; attention-seeking is minimal; sexualized presentation is absent (the Malice alter weaponized sexuality precisely *because* the host self-state forbids it — diagnostic in the opposite direction). Excluded.

### D. Dissociative Identity Disorder — RULED OUT

The Malice episode is the only candidate phenomenon and fails DID criteria:
- The alter was externally induced by the Hate-Monger / Psycho-Man, not endogenously formed.
- No history of switching outside the precipitated episode.
- No childhood-onset alter system.
- Integration achieved and sustained.
- No amnestic barriers in ordinary functioning.

Correctly classified as a **trauma-related dissociative episode, iatrogenically/adversarially triggered, in a substrate primed by chronic repression**. Not DID.

### E. Major Depressive Disorder — RULED OUT (current); historically not documented at threshold

No discrete episode meeting full DSM criteria in canonical record. Subthreshold dysthymic features previously noted; do not warrant MDD diagnosis.

### F. Generalized Anxiety Disorder — RULED OUT

Worry is domain-specific (family, children, ethical exposure), not free-floating. Somatic anxiety symptoms (muscle tension, sleep disturbance) are present but trauma-coded rather than GAD-coded. Subject does not meet criteria.

### G. Substance Use Disorder — RULED OUT

Strongly negative. Notably, subject's abstemiousness is itself a clinical datum — adult children of alcoholics often divide into mirror-of-parent and inverse-of-parent presentations; subject is unambiguously the latter. Vigilance around Johnny's substance and behavioral risk profile is consistent.

### H. Codependence (clinical sense) — RULED OUT, with qualification

She enables. She also confronts and exits when limits are exceeded. Clinical codependence requires the inability to set or enforce limits; subject can and does. The *appearance* of codependence is the residue of the ACoA loyalty pattern, not a distinct condition.

### I. Munchausen by Proxy / Factitious Disorder spectrum — RULED OUT

Mentioned only because some clinicians reflexively consider it in mothers of medically complex children. No evidence whatsoever; subject has consistently sought *to prevent* medical complications in her children, not engineer them. Trivially excluded.

### J. Acquired Sociopathy / Trauma-Induced Antisocial Features — RULED OUT

Considered because of the subject's documented capacity to rupture opposing combatants' internal organs via force-field pressure — a capability she has used. The act is not antisocial: it is deployed under specific ethical conditions, with restraint, and is followed by appropriate negative affect. No callousness, no remorse deficit, no instrumental aggression. Excluded.

### K. Erotomania / Pathological Idealization — RULED OUT (re: Reed)

The early attachment to Reed at age twelve was an idealization, but it has been reality-tested across sixty years with appropriate disillusionment and re-equilibration. The relationship is now substantially mutual. Not erotomanic.

---

## IV. Comorbidity Structure

The active conditions are not independent. They form a **coherent post-traumatic constellation rooted in early loss and parentification**, with the following relational geometry:

- *Persistent Complex Bereavement* supplies the affective baseline (low-grade chronic mourning).
- *PTSD residue* supplies the threat-discrimination architecture (hypervigilance to family endangerment).
- *ACoA phenotype* supplies the interpersonal operating system (over-functioning, loyalty-to-fault, vigilance toward impulsive intimates).
- *Subclinical dysthymic substrate* supplies the affective ceiling (joy is muted; satisfaction is duty-coded).

These conditions reinforce one another but also stabilize one another — the ACoA over-functioning provides a behavioral scaffold that prevents bereavement and PTSD from disorganizing daily function. This is **maladaptive in the long term and adaptive in the present**. Removing the scaffold without replacement would risk acute decompensation.

---

## V. Course Over Time

**Phase 1 (childhood–spaceflight):** Acute trauma encoding; parentification consolidates; primary attachment object selected (Reed) along the template the trauma produced.

**Phase 2 (1961–1973, Lee/Kirby through Franklin lobotomy):** Maximal suppression. Subclinical dysthymia, prodromal dissociative architecture. First rupture (Franklin lobotomy) is the watershed: the first time subject acted against the system to defend a family member from a family member.

**Phase 3 (1973–1984, strain era through stillbirth):** Increasing affective leakage. Force-field power expansion is the somatic correlate of the rage finding a route. The stillbirth (FF #267) is the unintegrated trauma that primes the Malice substrate.

**Phase 4 (1984–1986, Byrne era / Malice integration):** Acute decompensation in the form of an externally precipitated dissociative episode. Forced integration. Identity reorganization. The Invisible Girl–to–Invisible Woman renaming is symbolic of a real intrapsychic event.

**Phase 5 (1986–2006, post-Byrne to Civil War):** Consolidation. Earned-secure attachment overlay develops. Ethical confidence accrues. Generativity expressed through Valeria, Future Foundation seeds.

**Phase 6 (2006–present):** Mature integration. Capable of structural defection (Civil War), planetary diplomacy, pedagogical authority. Underlying wounds remain visible in geometry but no longer dictate behavior.

The trajectory is one of **genuine therapeutic progress accomplished outside any therapeutic frame**, accelerated by adversity that functioned, accidentally, as exposure-and-integration treatment.

---

## VI. Prognostic Notes and Decompensation Risk

**Stable as long as:** Family system remains intact; she retains agentive role; combat occurs at the cosmic register her capability matches; Reed continues the post-Civil War trend of treating her judgment as decisive on ethical questions.

**At risk if:**
- Loss of a child. The compensation structure was built around the surviving children. A loss would likely produce a Major Depressive Episode with high suicide risk (low base-rate for the subject but high relative jump) and possible re-emergence of dissociative defenses.
- Reed's death or permanent incapacity. Would produce acute grief reaction, almost certainly survivable given current resources, but with substantial risk of identity-organizing crisis given how much of her selfhood was constructed around the relationship.
- Johnny's death, particularly substance- or recklessness-related. Would activate the ACoA wound at its deepest layer.
- Forced confrontation with the consent conditions of her original spaceflight, marriage, or motherhood. Currently defended against by retrospective endorsement; if breached, would produce a destabilizing reassessment.
- A second possession event of the Malice type. The substrate is integrated but not absent; a sufficiently sophisticated adversary could exploit it.

**Recommended (hypothetical) intervention:** Subject would benefit from formal grief work specifically targeting the maternal and perinatal losses; from a relational therapy with Reed that surfaces the early-attachment power asymmetry; and from the structural acknowledgement, by her family, of the labor she has performed silently for six decades. She will not seek any of these. She does not believe she requires them. She is approximately seventy percent correct about this, which is the highest accuracy figure achievable from her position.

---

## VII. Diagnostic Summary

**Active:**
- Persistent Complex Bereavement Disorder, chronic, partially compensated.
- PTSD, chronic, in partial remission, with historical dissociative features.
- Adult Children of Alcoholics phenotype (operational, not coded).
- Subclinical persistent depressive features (trace).

**Historical, integrated:**
- Trauma-induced dissociative episode (Malice), externally precipitated, resolved.

**Ruled out:**
- DPD, BPD, HPD, DID, MDD, GAD, SUD, clinical codependence, Munchausen by proxy, acquired sociopathy, erotomania.

**Overarching formulation:**
Subject is a high-functioning trauma survivor whose adaptations have, across six decades, evolved from pure survival defenses into a substantially integrated and generative adult character structure. The residue of the original wounds is visible in her relational geometry, her somatic-symbolic power expression, and her threat-discrimination thresholds, but does not produce active disorder. She is, in the most precise sense the discipline can offer, **a case of post-traumatic growth that has not entirely escaped the post-traumatic substrate from which it grew** — and the gap between what she has accomplished and what she will allow herself to acknowledge accomplishing is the last clinical fact of the file.


## Behavioral Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION VI: BEHAVIORAL ATLAS

## Subject: Susan Storm Richards
## Scope: Total catalog of observed and inferable behavioral signatures across all known states, 1961–present. Cross-referenced where canon permits; otherwise reconstructed from longitudinal pattern.

---

## A. BASELINE / CALM STATE

### Postural Signature
Subject in repose carries her weight slightly forward on the balls of the feet — a vestige of modeling training carried into adulthood, never lost. Shoulders held back without performative effort; spine long. When seated, she does not slump even in private quarters; the one observed exception is on the Baxter Building common-room couch with Franklin or Valeria physically against her, where she will let her shoulders round forward over the child. This is the **only domestic posture in which she fully surrenders verticality**, and it is diagnostic of where her actual rest-state lives.

### Hand Behavior
Hands at rest are visible — palms down on table, folded loosely in lap, never tucked away. Subject who can disappear by reflex makes a point of leaving her hands seen. When thinking, the right hand will rise to touch the base of the throat (not the collarbone, not the sternum — the suprasternal notch), a gesture inherited from her mother per the rare flashback panels (FF Annual #1 visual quotation). When listening to Reed lecture, the index and middle finger of the left hand will tap once, twice, against the opposite wrist — **a privately metronomic count of how long he has been talking**.

### Vocal Baseline
Mid-register, unhurried, with terminal consonants fully articulated — the residue of her aunt's New York middle-class enunciation drilling. She does not uptalk. Statements end down. Questions are unambiguous. When she is genuinely uncertain she will *say* "I'm not sure," rather than perform uncertainty prosodically. Volume floor is lower than the room's; people lean toward her, which is the desired effect.

### Eye Behavior
Holds gaze longer than the American conversational norm — approximately 1.5x average duration on the speaker, with brief, deliberate breaks downward and to the left (recall-quadrant), almost never upward (which would read as performance). When she is being condescended to, the gaze does not narrow; it *steadies*. The blink rate drops. Veteran observers (Ben, Wyatt Wingfoot, T'Challa) have learned to register the blink-rate drop as the actual warning sign rather than any verbal cue.

### Power Idle
Invisibility is **off** by default in safe environments — a deliberate choice, given how natural a default-on state would be for her. The decision to remain visible is itself a behavior: she chose, somewhere in the Byrne years, to stop using invisibility as a hiding place. Force-field generation is unconsciously active at a sub-threshold level — a phenomenon observed by Reed in instrumentation (a faint persistent psionic carrier signature, ~3 cm off the skin surface) that she herself is unaware of. **Her body is permanently shielded at a level below her awareness.** It is the somatic correlate of a woman who has never since adolescence felt fully safe.

### Domestic Micro-Habits
- Will not enter a room without scanning entry/exit lines first; this is so habituated she does not register doing it.
- Touches doorframes lightly with the fingertips on passing through — a tactile re-anchoring tic, increased in frequency during high-stress weeks.
- Coffee, not tea; black, one sugar; mug held two-handed regardless of temperature. The two-handed grip is a self-hug substitute and predates the powers.
- Reads physical books, not screens, when actually trying to think.
- Keeps a small framed photograph (her mother, c. 1950s) in the bedside drawer rather than on top of the dresser. Out of sight, within reach.

---

## B. SOCIAL / DIPLOMATIC STATE

### With Strangers of Status (heads of state, Atlantean court, Wakandan diplomats)
Subject deploys what Atlantean protocol records describe as "the unbroken courtesy" — a register in which she neither flatters nor flatters-down. She uses given names and titles correctly on first attempt without prompting (she studies); she will not interrupt; she will hold a question in queue across a full diplomatic round and ask it last, by which point it has reframed the entire conversation. Observable tells: she takes notes by hand on a small folio, not for the content (she remembers it) but as a **deliberate signal of attentiveness** to the speaker. The notes are later discarded.

### With Strangers of No Status (children, civilians, service staff)
Posture drops half an inch. Voice softens by approximately 10%. Eye contact lengthens further. Will learn names of doormen, cooks, security at the Baxter Building and use them; will remember a junior staffer's child's name from a year prior. This is not cultivated affect — it is the **default she suppresses upward** in rooms where she needs to be perceived as Authority.

### Group Tactical Briefings
She speaks fourth or fifth, never first. By the time she speaks, three or four bad ideas have been aired and silently catalogued. Her statement will (a) name the actual stakes in a single sentence, (b) eliminate two of the bad ideas without naming them as bad, (c) propose a course of action that incorporates the salvageable element of someone else's contribution — usually the most junior person's, awarding them credit. **This is hostage-negotiator architecture deployed inside her own kitchen.**

---

## C. INTIMATE / PARTNERED STATE (with Reed)

### Proximity Behavior
She is the one who closes physical distance. Reed, left to himself, will work across a room from her for nine hours. She will arrive at his elbow, place a hand on his forearm — fingertips, not palm — and wait. The fingertip contact is calibrated: heavy enough to register through his abstraction, light enough not to seem demanding. He responds to it 80% of the time within twenty seconds; the other 20% she removes her hand without comment and tries again ninety minutes later. **The two-tries-then-disengage rule is iron.** She has never been observed begging for his attention. She has been observed leaving the room.

### Verbal Pattern
Calls him "Reed" in mixed company, "Reed" in front of the children, and — the diagnostic — *uses no nickname at all* in private. Where most long marriages develop a private vocative, theirs has not; or rather, hers for him has not. He calls her "Sue" or "darling"; she calls him by his given name in every register. Reading: she has never permitted herself the illusion that he is anything other than the specific, difficult person he is. **She loves him in full focus.**

### Conflict Initiation
Subject does not raise grievances at point of injury. They are filed, dated internally, and raised in a controlled window — typically late evening, after children are asleep, in their shared workspace rather than the bedroom (the bedroom is preserved as non-combat terrain — a rule unverbalized but enforced by her). Opening sentence template: "I need you to hear something." Not "we need to talk." Not "I'm upset." A directive to *listen*, which forecloses his reflex to problem-solve. He has learned, over decades, to put down the work.

### Sexual / Affectional Tells (inferable)
Public physical affection is restrained — a hand at the small of his back, brief; no extended embraces. Private behavior, per the few canonical glimpses, is the inverse: she is the initiator more often than not, which tracks with the proximity-closer pattern in all domains. She is the active partner in a relationship with a man whose attention is the prize and whose body is, often literally, somewhere else.

### Tells of Genuine Contentment with Him
- She hums while working in his lab (he has learned to identify the songs — pre-1962 standards, her mother's repertoire).
- She permits him to ramble for longer than her usual tolerance and the wrist-tap does not appear.
- She removes her shoes.

---

## D. INTIMATE / SIBLING STATE (with Johnny)

### Voice Shift
Drops half an octave; loses the diplomatic polish; New York vowels return. With Johnny she sounds like the seventeen-year-old who raised him. She uses "Johnny" for routine address, "Jonathan" for serious correction (which lands like a slap precisely because their father was the last person to use it), and a wordless inhalation through the nose for "I see what you did and we will discuss it."

### Touch Pattern
Will straighten his collar, brush hair off his forehead, thumb a smudge off his cheek — at thirty-eight, forty-five, fifty. He tolerates this from no one else and protests only ritually. The touch is **not maternal performance; it is genuinely automatic**, and she has tried twice in published record to consciously stop and failed within a week.

### Conflict Pattern with Johnny
Where with Reed she queues and files, with Johnny she lances immediately and loudly and is over it within the hour. She does not store grievances against him. The asymmetry is significant: Reed gets the controlled adult docket; Johnny gets the unmediated older-sister volume. **Johnny is the only person in her life with whom she fully behaves her age and below.**

---

## E. MATERNAL STATE (with Franklin, Valeria)

### Threat Vigilance
Constant, sub-conscious, environmentally indexed. Subject can be in deep conversation and will register her child's altered breathing pattern across a room. Head turn precedes the auditory event by a measurable fraction. With Franklin (reality-warper) and Valeria (intellect-of-Doom-tier), the vigilance has additional dimensions: she watches for **affective shifts that precede capability events** — Franklin's tells before an unconscious power surge, Valeria's micro-expressions before a manipulative cognitive maneuver. She has, with both children, the only consistently *unsuppressed* affect display in her behavioral repertoire.

### Discipline Pattern
Quiet voice, eye level, full attention, single statement of the problem, single statement of the expectation. No raised voice. No deferral to Reed ("wait until your father gets home" has never been used and would be received as betrayal by the child). She owns the disciplinary office and does not subcontract it.

### Tell of Maternal Fear
The fingertip-to-suprasternal-notch gesture becomes a full hand flat against the upper chest. She will not say "I'm scared." She has never said it in front of either child. The hand on the chest is the substitute and her family reads it.

---

## F. STRESS STATE (escalating)

### Tier 1 — Cognitive Load Without Threat
Wrist-tap surfaces. Coffee consumption doubles. Sentences shorten. Diplomatic register narrows — less small talk, more direct answers. She will start scheduling: writing lists, building agendas, imposing structure on the disorder. Sleep shortens by an hour at each end. She does not announce stress; she announces *plans*.

### Tier 2 — Interpersonal Strain (Reed disengagement, Johnny crisis, team friction)
Subject becomes geographically mobile within the building — moves rooms more often, takes meetings standing, paces the corridor outside the lab rather than entering. Touches doorframes more. Will go to a window and stand at it for two-to-six minutes at intervals; the window-standing is the closest she has to a meditative practice. Blink rate drops in conversation. Humor sharpens and acquires edges; she begins to **make jokes she would not have made the week before**, and the targets are usually Reed.

### Tier 3 — Sustained Acute Stress (multi-day crisis)
The autonomic force-field carrier signature thickens; ambient psionic field detectable to instrumentation at ~8 cm. Touch becomes selective — she will accept physical contact only from the children. Eats less; coffee replaces meals. The Storm-family insomnia pattern fully activates: she will be found in the lab at 0300, not working, *present*. She begins to ask Reed direct technical questions she already knows the answers to — a behavior whose function is to **force him to engage with her using his own register**, which is the only register that holds his attention under his own stress.

### Tier 4 — Crisis Threshold
Sentences drop to clauses. Movement becomes economical and predictive — she is already where she needs to be before the threat materializes. Invisibility deploys reflexively as a *scouting* mode rather than a hiding mode (she goes invisible, observes, returns). Force-field constructs begin appearing pre-attack as architecture: cordoning corridors, separating combatants, sealing rooms. She gives orders that Reed and Ben obey without negotiation, and afterwards no one comments on the role reversal.

### Tier 5 — Decision to Defect / Leave
Behavioral signature: she becomes *more* polite, not less. Voice softens. Eye contact lengthens. She thanks people for things. **This is the most dangerous behavioral state subject exhibits**, and is the published precursor to her departures (the Franklin-lobotomy walkout; the Civil War defection; minor recorded separations across the Bronze Age). When Susan Richards begins speaking to her husband with the courtesy due a stranger, the marriage is forty-eight hours from rupture and he has, by long pattern, that long to recognize it.

---

## G. THREAT / COMBAT STATE

### Pre-Engagement
A single deep breath through the nose, exhaled through the mouth — the only consistently observable somatic preparation. Hands open at the sides, fingers spread. She does not assume a fighting stance; her stance is the same as her conversational stance, which is itself a tell: she does not need to telegraph readiness because **the readiness is structural**.

### Engagement Logic
Defense before offense, always. First constructs are perimeter: separate civilians from combat, isolate the hostile, deny terrain. Second-tier constructs are restraint: bubbles, pillars, planes. Offensive force is third resort and is **calibrated, never maximal**. She has demonstrated planet-scale shielding and surgical intra-cranial pressure application; she uses neither in 95% of engagements. The withholding is doctrinal. She does not want her opponents — or her family — to know the ceiling.

### Tells of Lethal Intent (rare)
When she has decided to seriously injure or kill, the behavioral signature is *silence*. She stops giving commands. She stops calling out positions. She does not warn. The construct appears inside the opponent without preamble. Ben has identified this pattern in private conversation with Reed and neither man has raised it with her. **She knows they know and has not addressed it either.**

### Post-Engagement
Subject immediately walks the field — counts bodies (allied and civilian), checks pulses, identifies wounded. She does this before debriefing, before reporting, before resting. Then she finds her brother and physically touches him (shoulder, arm) to confirm he is intact. Then Reed. Then she sits down. The order is invariant.

---

## H. INTIMACY / VULNERABILITY STATE

### Conditions Under Which She Will Reveal Distress
- Alone with Ben Grimm. He is the **only adult to whom she has wept in published record without external precipitant**. She does not ask for advice; she sits next to him and the gravity of his physical mass licenses her own collapse. He does not speak first.
- Alone with Alicia Masters. The conversations are sister-coded and the topics are usually Reed.
- Alone with her children, *only* when they have already cried and she is comforting them — she will permit her own tears to accompany theirs, never to precede them.

### Conditions Under Which She Will Not
- In front of Reed. The single largest behavioral asymmetry of the marriage. She has cried *near* him; not *to* him.
