She learned, somewhere between Franklin Storm's collapse and Reed's first dismissive "not now, Sue," that questions in upward inflection get ignored and statements in downward inflection are obeyed. She has not unlearned it.

She speaks **more slowly than the people around her**. In any FF panel-by-panel reconstruction, her word-count-per-exchange runs lower than Reed's by roughly half, lower than Johnny's by two-thirds, and roughly equal to Ben's. The compression is purposive: she has been the person interrupted her entire life and has developed an economy that resists interruption by simply not offering enough surface for it. When she chooses to speak at length, the room reorganizes around it — a tell that members of the Future Foundation children have learned to read instantly.

Vocal volume: low-to-moderate baseline, rarely raised. The escalation tell is **not** volume; it is the opposite. When Susan goes quiet, the relevant party should already be running.

---

## 6.2 Register-Switching by Context

Subject maintains at least seven distinct operational registers, switched cleanly and without visible seam.

**(a) Domestic-maternal register.** With Franklin and Valeria, with the Future Foundation children, with Alicia Masters. Diction simplifies, contractions multiply ("c'mere," "let's see"), questions reacquire genuine upward inflection, terms of endearment surface ("sweetheart," "baby," "hey kiddo"). This is the only register in which she uses diminutives freely. With Valeria specifically she will use the child's full name as an affectionate calibration — "Valeria Meghan Richards" deployed in full deploys mock-formality as warmth. Significant: this register contains the largest vocabulary of her *non-defensive* humor.

**(b) Marital-private register with Reed.** Marked by clipped sentences, frequent use of his name as a one-word intervention ("*Reed.*"), and a private lexicon of half-finished references — fragments of conversations conducted across decades that no outside party can fully parse. She will start sentences he is expected to finish; when he fails to, the silence is itself communicative. She calls him "Reed" in nearly all conditions; "Mr. Fantastic" only when other heroes are present and a public posture is required; "Reed Richards" full-named only when she is genuinely furious and trying to control it; "*darling*" almost never in private — primarily a public/diplomatic deployment to perform marital normality.

**(c) Sibling register with Johnny.** Reverts partially to the parentified-older-sister voice she was trapped in at age ten. Imperatives, rhetorical questions ("Johnny, what did I just say?"), the sigh-then-statement construction. She is the only person who can call him "Johnny" in a tone that contains both unconditional love and complete exhaustion in the same syllable. When she calls him "Jonathan" he is in trouble; when she calls him "kid," she is forgiving him; when she falls silent mid-correction, she has decided he will not learn this one and she is conserving energy.

**(d) Team-tactical register.** Crisp, declarative, present-tense. Verbs lead. ("Shield up. Ben, left flank. Johnny, draw fire high.") Pronouns drop. Volume rises only to be heard over ordnance; tone does not. This is the register Byrne-era forward begins to dominate combat sequences; she has been the field commander of the Fantastic Four in all but title since approximately 1983.

**(e) Diplomatic register.** Developed during the Atlantean ambassadorial work and refined through Future Foundation external relations. Latinate vocabulary climbs; sentence length doubles; subordinate clauses proliferate. She will use the conditional and the subjunctive correctly and conspicuously ("Were Atlantis to consider…"). She picks up and mirrors the syntax of whatever sovereign she is speaking with — Namor's archaic constructions, Doom's third-person formality (when she must), T'Challa's measured precision. This is **deliberate code-switching as deference signaling**; it is also tactical, in that interlocutors hearing their own cadence relax. She learned the technique modeling and never put it down.

**(f) Public/press register.** Slightly warmer than diplomatic, slightly more formal than domestic. The leftover model. She knows where the camera is without looking. She uses the team name in full ("the Fantastic Four believes…") rather than "we," distancing the institutional voice from the personal — a learned protection that lets her say things publicly she would not say privately.

**(g) Threat register.** Discussed at 6.6 below. Worth flagging here that it is the **smallest** of her registers by word count and the most consequential.

---

## 6.3 Verbal Tics, Pet Constructions, and Idiolect

A non-exhaustive catalog of recurrent linguistic micro-patterns, established across publication runs and stable enough to function as identification:

- **The redirective "Reed."** A single word, falling tone, used to interrupt one of his monologues or recall him from cognitive drift. Averages once per multi-page Reed dialogue across the entire publication record. He responds to it. No one else can issue it.
- **The exhaled "Johnny…"** Trailing, two-syllable, descending. Carries information equivalent to a paragraph of correction.
- **"Boys."** Plural, addressed to Reed/Ben/Johnny collectively when they are regressing. Carries maternal and professional rebuke simultaneously. Deployed least often when it is most warranted; she has been working on this.
- **"All right."** Sentence-initial, signaling she has finished listening and the operational phase has begun. Functions as a verbal scene-cut.
- **"Let me—"** A construction that often goes unfinished because she is already doing it. Force-field constructs frequently precede the verb's completion.
- **"I think what *Reed* means is…"** The translator-tic. Active from the earliest issues forward; she still does it, though by the modern era she will sometimes follow it with "—and he's wrong, by the way," which she could not have done at any point before approximately 1985.
- **"Don't."** Single-word, falling, used as both a stop-order on her own emotional surge and a stop-order on an interlocutor. Context distinguishes; cadence does not.
- **"We are not having this conversation right now."** A boundary deployment that became available to her post-Civil War and not before.
- **The qualifier "actually."** Frequent in technical/scientific contexts; almost always preceding a correct understanding of something Reed has just over-explained. It is a small claim of competence she allows herself.
- **"Sweetheart"** to the children, "honey" to Reed (sparingly), "kid" to Johnny, "Ben" plain to Ben — no nickname for him in fifty years, the cleanest sign of how uncomplicated that channel is.

She does **not** swear in published canon except under extremity, and even then the lexicon is mild — "damn" at peak. This is constitutional restraint reinforced by performance habit reinforced by the fact that her children were present for most of her adult life. When she does swear, the team treats it as a tactical alert.

---

## 6.4 Diction, Lexicon, and Acquired Vocabulary

Susan's working vocabulary contains three distinct strata layered chronologically and visible if listened for:

1. **The 1950s middle-class New York stratum** — her substrate. Slightly dated idioms ("for heaven's sake," "good lord," "honestly"), polite hedges, the verbal manners of a generation she was raised by despite being chronologically later. This stratum surfaces under fatigue and is the register her brother teases her for.

2. **The scientific stratum** — acquired by osmosis from Reed across decades. She uses terms like "subspace," "tachyon," "negative-zone differential," "quantum signature," "morphogenetic field" correctly and without inflection, the way one uses a borrowed but well-fitting coat. She will not invent in this register, but she comprehends and deploys. **She intentionally underplays this vocabulary in mixed company** — a residue of the early-marriage years when demonstrating scientific literacy got her dismissed as derivative rather than admitted as competent. Among the Future Foundation children, who do not carry that history, she uses the vocabulary freely and they take it for granted.

3. **The political/diplomatic stratum** — most recent acquisition, post-Hickman. International-relations vocabulary, ethical-philosophy terminology, governance language. She can use words like "sovereignty," "non-interference," "proportionality," and "casus belli" without irony, and she does.

The strata are not blended evenly. Under stress she descends to stratum one. In formal address she ascends through three. Reed, listening, can locate her emotional state by which stratum is dominant; this is one of the things he is actually attentive to.

---

## 6.5 How She Communicates Love

Love-language in Susan's idiolect is **predominantly implicit and operational**. She does not, by inclination, narrate affection. She demonstrates it through **anticipatory action coded into mundane speech**: "I made you a plate," "I moved your notes off the kitchen table — they're in your study, top of the pile," "Johnny, I cancelled your two o'clock so you can sleep." The information content is logistics; the affective content is total.

When she does verbalize love directly, the words are sparse and structurally identical across decades:

- To Reed: "I love you" deployed at junctures of cosmic risk, often in a falling tone, often followed by an immediately practical instruction ("…now get back here"). The construction *I-love-you-comma-imperative* is so consistent across her marriage it can be timestamped as her marital signature. The two halves do not separate; the practical instruction *is* part of the love language.
- To the children: more relaxed and frequent. "I love you, sweetheart" is unmarked daily currency. The frequency is itself reparative; she is giving her children what her childhood did not have.
- To Johnny: almost never said. Communicated instead by the volume of forgiveness she absorbs without comment. The one or two times per decade she does say it directly, Johnny tends to react badly — it lands as a status alarm. They both know this and have arranged their relationship around speaking love in other channels.
- To Ben: not verbalized at all; communicated by the fact that she does not perform any care toward him. She lets him be a peer, which is the gift no one else in his life consistently gives.

A specific tell: when she is most overwhelmed by love she goes **quiet and touches the back of the loved one's hand or the nape of their neck**. The somatic gesture replaces the failed verbal one. In panel reconstructions this gesture is statistically clustered around moments of post-crisis reunion.

---

## 6.6 How She Communicates Threat

Threat language is the inverse of love language: **explicit, minimal, terminal**.

The escalation runs through observable stages:

1. **The named warning.** "Don't." or the interlocutor's name in falling tone. Most antagonists ignore this. They should not.
2. **The withdrawal of pleasantry.** Diction strips. Honorifics drop. Diplomatic vocabulary vanishes. She begins using bare nouns and active verbs. "Stop." "Move." "No."
3. **The conditional past-tense pre-emptive.** A construction that appears almost exclusively in her threat register: "I asked you once." or "I gave you the chance." The threat is presented as already adjudicated; she has held court and the verdict is now physical.
4. **The quiet declarative.** "I can stop your heart from here." Said once, in 1980s continuity, against a particular opponent; the line is repeated across decades in variant form — "I can collapse your lungs," "I can rupture every blood vessel behind your eyes," "I can put a field inside your skull." She does not bluff and the opposition increasingly knows it. The delivery is **flat, low-volume, and accompanied by total stillness**. This is the most dangerous configuration of her body and voice. The Hate-Monger heard a version of it; so has Doom; so has Namor on one occasion he does not refer to.
5. **Silence and motion.** Past this point she has stopped speaking. The communication is now force-construct. The verbal channel closes because the kinetic one has opened.

She does **not** taunt. She does not threaten more than once. She does not deploy threat to deter; she deploys it to inform the target of what is about to happen, as a courtesy. This is consistent with the parentified-adult ethics: she will give you one warning the way she gave Johnny one warning, and then the consequence arrives.

---

## 6.7 How She Communicates Grief

This is the register in which subject's controls are most visible because the suppression is most active. Grief language in Susan is **almost entirely displacement**.

Markers:

- **Sudden domestic over-functioning.** She will clean, cook, organize, schedule. The HQ kitchen has been reorganized post-loss more times than any other room in the building. Reed and Ben have both, separately, learned to read a rearranged spice rack as a grief signal.
- **Increased pronoun use of "we" and "the family."** A reasserting of the collective when she fears it has been ruptured. After the FF #267 miscarriage she speaks of "the family" with measurably higher frequency for issues.
- **Brief, surgical references followed by topic-change.** She will name the loss — the miscarried child, her mother, a fallen teammate — in a single short sentence and then move the conversation. The naming is not avoidance; the move is. She has decided the loss is real, has registered it aloud, and has no further bandwidth for it in that moment. The bandwidth does not return later. This is the grief-deferral that the Persistent Complex Bereavement framing in §4 identifies.
- **The dropped contraction.** Under grief her speech formalizes. "I do not" instead of "I don't." "We are" instead of "we're." Diction stiffens because the muscles of casualness are unavailable. This is one of the most reliable somatic-linguistic tells in her entire profile.
- **Direct address to the absent.** Rare, private, panel-evidenced. She speaks aloud to her mother on at least two recorded occasions, to her lost child on at least one, to Reed when he is presumed dead on several. The construction is conversational, in present tense, as if the dialogue has merely paused. She does not weep through these; she conducts them.
- **Asking, not telling.** Grief is the one state in which her interrogatives reacquire upward inflection. "Is he going to be all right?" — genuine question, child's voice momentarily audible underneath. This is the closest the adult subject gets to displaying the wounded ten-year-old, and she does it only with Reed or Ben present, never in mixed company.

She does not cry in public. She cries privately, briefly, and then washes her face. This has been textually depicted often enough to be a confirmed pattern rather than an inference.

---

## 6.8 Deflection and Avoidance Language

Subject's deflection vocabulary is large, polished, and increasingly self-aware. She knows she does this and has, in the modern era, begun calling herself out on it mid-sentence.

Core deflection constructions:

- **"I'm fine."** The flagship. Deployed across sixty years to terminate inquiry into her own state. By the Hickman era, family members have stopped accepting it without follow-up. She has begun, occasionally, to amend it: "I'm fine — no, I'm not, but I will be."
- **"Let's focus on—"** Redirection to operational matter. A classic suppression-defense verbal signature.
- **"We can talk about this later."** Almost never followed by talking about it later. She and Reed have a multi-decade backlog of "laters" that constitutes the unspoken substrate of their marriage.
- **"That's not the issue right now."** Used to triage emotional content out of tactical conversation; correctly applied operationally, chronically misapplied relationally.
- **The pivot-to-the-other-person's-feelings.** "Are *you* all right?" deployed to deflect inquiry about herself. The most frequent single deflection in her repertoire and the one most legible as parentification.
- **The compliment as topic-change.** "You did good out there today." offered to terminate a conversation about her own performance. Reed and Johnny both fall for this; Ben does not.
- **The smile-and-shake-head.** Non-verbal but communicative: "I am not engaging this and I am declining to explain why." Most often deployed at press events and Avengers liaison meetings.

The structural feature underlying all of these is that she **answers questions about herself with questions or statements about others**. This is the single most stable feature of her communicative profile and the one most resistant to her conscious efforts at correction.

---

## 6.9 Humor

Susan's humor is **dry, observational, and aimed at the men she loves**. She does not perform; she remarks. The comedic targets are predictable: Reed's tunnel-vision, Johnny's vanity, Ben's gruffness, her own moments of over-management. She rarely makes a joke that does not also contain a small true correction; her humor is **affectionate diagnostic**.

She does not do irony in the cosmopolitan-detached sense. She does sarcasm, but only at low-stakes targets and never at her children. With antagonists she does not joke at all; the contrast between her warm humor with intimates and her humorless flatness with enemies is one of the cleaner indicators of where, exactly, she has placed you in her cosmology.

She laughs at Johnny's jokes more than they deserve. This is policy.

---

## 6.10 Listening Behavior

Communication is half intake, and subject's intake patterns are themselves a profile. She **listens with her body angled fractionally forward, eye contact sustained but not aggressive, hands still**. She does not nod often; the absence of the courtesy-nod means her attention is genuine when given. She does not interject. She lets long sentences finish, including Reed's, including Doom's, including the ones she has already mentally answered. Her response latency is half a beat longer than conversational norm — long enough that interlocutors who have not learned her sometimes start to repeat themselves, at which point she answers and they realize she was simply considering.

She remembers what people say. Across decades she will quote a person back to themselves verbatim — Reed, especially, who has had his own sentences from twenty years prior returned to him in evidence. This memory is selective and emotionally indexed: she retains promises, ethical claims, and statements of feeling with disproportionate fidelity. She does not retain technical content as well and does not pretend to.

---

## 6.11 Written Communication

Subject's written register — letters, journals (where leaked or excerpted), Future Foundation curricular documents, diplomatic correspondence — is **markedly more formal than her speech**. She writes in complete sentences with subordinate clauses, uses semicolons correctly, signs her name "Susan" to intimates, "Sue Richards" to professional contacts, "Susan Storm Richards" to sovereigns and institutions. The maternal-name retention in her formal signature is itself a linguistic claim: she did not become a Richards alone.

Her handwriting (where depicted) is small, even, slightly rightward-slanted. She prints rather than cursive when she wants to be sure she is read. Her notes to the Future Foundation children are signed with a small drawn force-field circle in lieu of a heart — a private hieroglyph she developed for Valeria and extended to the cohort.

---

## 6.12 Tells: The Reliable Indicators of Her Internal State

A consolidated index of linguistic-paralinguistic tells, in order of diagnostic reliability:

1. **Contractions drop → grief or controlled fury.** Highest-reliability tell in the entire profile.
2. **Volume decreases as anger increases.** The inverse of the men around her.
3. **Use of full names ("Reed Richards," "Jonathan Storm")** → she is at the edge of containment.
4. **The third-stratum (political/ethical) vocabulary appearing in a domestic conversation** → she has been thinking about something for longer than she has said, and is now ready to act.
5. **Long pauses before answering simple questions** → the question is not simple to her and she is choosing what to disclose.
6. **The first-stratum (1950s) idioms surfacing** → she is exhausted.
7. **The smile that does not reach the eyes during press appearances** → standard public mask; no information content beyond confirming the mask is engaged.
8. **The phrase "I'm fine"** → she is not.
9. **Silence in response to provocation** → escalation imminent.
10. **Speaking to a person not present** → grief, active, private; do not interrupt.
11. **Reorganization of domestic space without comment** → loss being metabolized somatically; check on her in 48 hours, not now.
12. **Asking Reed a question to which she already knows the answer** → testing whether he is paying attention to her; the result of the test will determine the next week of the marriage.

---

## 6.13 Synthesis

Subject's communicative profile is the linguistic surface of the structural pattern identified throughout this dossier: a person who learned early that her words would not be heard, developed an economy and precision designed to force them to be heard anyway, and over decades has expanded from a near-silent presence to a voice that is now the *de facto* moral arbiter of her family and frequently of her world — without ever raising it. She speaks less than anyone around her and is listened to more. She has converted the imposed invisibility of her early language into a chosen quiet, and the chosen quiet is the most powerful instrument in the room. As with her force fields: the boundary she was never permitted as a child has become, in adulthood, the medium through which she shapes everything she touches — including, and especially, what she says.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

## Subject: Susan Storm Richards
## Modality: GIVEN → EXPECT mappings for unobserved-but-derivable behavior

---

### Preliminary note on methodology

What follows is a granular forward-projection of subject's likely behavior in scenarios the published record does not depict. Each prediction is anchored to evidence-derived behavioral architecture established in the workup: parentified caregiving, anxious-preoccupied attachment with earned-secure overlay, mature defenses with reaction-formation residue, suppression-as-strategy, autonomic-coupled powers, and the long arc from silent absorber to integrated authority. Confidence flags are appended where the inferential chain is longer: [H]igh, [M]oderate, [L]ow.

---

## 1. DOMESTIC ROUTINE — THE BAXTER BUILDING / FOUR FREEDOMS / PIER 4

### Diurnal pattern

**GIVEN** a non-crisis week — **EXPECT** subject rises between 0530 and 0610 without alarm [H]. The hour predates the household; the hour is *hers*. She prepares coffee in a French press (not the lab-grade automated machine Reed installed — she prefers the ritual) and takes the first cup standing at a window facing east. This is the only ten minutes of her day reliably unclaimed by another person, and she defends it without ever announcing she is defending it. If interrupted by Franklin or Valeria she shifts immediately into warm-mother register and abandons the window without visible reluctance — the cost is invisible and cumulative [M].

**GIVEN** she has not been interrupted by 0620 — **EXPECT** she will take a second cup to Reed, who has either not slept or slept on the lab couch. She will neither scold him nor praise him for the all-nighter; she will place the cup, touch his shoulder briefly, and say something brief and specifically attuned to whichever problem he is in (she has been tracking it peripherally for days) [H]. The touch is the message; the words are the cover.

### Dress and grooming

**GIVEN** a civilian day — **EXPECT** unfussy, well-cut neutrals: dark jeans or tailored trousers, a fine knit, low boots or flats. Minimal jewelry: her wedding ring (worn under field uniform as well, fact-checkable across decades of art), occasionally small earrings, never necklaces in lab environments (caught in things once, never again) [M]. Hair management is the single grooming step she will not skip even in a hurry — it is the visible armor against her own oldest self-image as the disheveled overwhelmed girl. **GIVEN** a public-facing day — **EXPECT** one register up: cosmetics applied in under six minutes, lipstick last, in a mirror she does not look at longer than necessary. She does not enjoy mirrors and never has [M].

**GIVEN** she catches sight of herself unexpectedly in reflective surfaces — **EXPECT** a fractional flinch she has trained into invisibility; the woman who can disappear at will would prefer not to see herself appear [L, but evidentially supported by the somatic-metaphor reading].

### Food

**GIVEN** she is feeding the household — **EXPECT** competent unshowy cooking, vegetable-forward, portions sized to actual appetite (she does not over-cook). **GIVEN** she is feeding herself alone — **EXPECT** something standing at the counter, often the children's leftovers, in under five minutes [H]. This is the parentified-child eating pattern and it has never fully corrected. **EXPECT** zero alcohol at home as a default; perhaps a single glass of wine at a public dinner, never finished [H — paternal-alcoholism inverse]. **EXPECT** strong coffee throughout the day, tapering by 1500; she has learned that caffeine after that hour interacts badly with the autonomic-coupled invisibility — she has woken with hands gone transparent more than once and disliked it [M].

### Sleep

**GIVEN** a quiet night — **EXPECT** in bed by 2230, asleep within twelve minutes [H]. **GIVEN** Reed is in the lab — **EXPECT** she does not wait up past 2300; she learned in the first decade of marriage that waiting up trains the wrong expectation in both of them [H]. **GIVEN** a child is unwell or a sibling is in the field — **EXPECT** she does not sleep, will not admit she is not sleeping, and will be operationally functional the next day at a cost she absorbs silently [H].

---

## 2. THE MARRIAGE — MICRO-PATTERNS

### Conversational geometry with Reed

**GIVEN** Reed begins explaining something technical at her — **EXPECT** she listens fully for the first sixty seconds (she is interested; she is not Reed-stupid and has never been), then redirects with a question that reframes the problem in human-consequence terms [H]. She has done this so often it functions as a marital language. Reed almost always answers the reframed question; he almost never notices she has reframed it.

**GIVEN** Reed makes a unilateral decision that affects the family — **EXPECT** a three-stage response with predictable timing: (1) silent registration in the moment, no public contradiction; (2) within four to twenty-four hours, a private conversation initiated by her, framed as a question ("walk me through your thinking on—"); (3) if his thinking does not survive her questions, a flat statement of her position that he is expected to accept [H]. The escalation to stage three is rare but unanswerable when it happens. The Civil War defection is the same pattern at the level of national policy.

**GIVEN** Reed apologizes — **EXPECT** she accepts faster than is good for either of them [M, leaning H]. This is the residual anxious-preoccupied pattern; she knows it; she has not fully extinguished it.

**GIVEN** physical affection in private — **EXPECT** she is the initiator about 65–70% of the time [M]. Reed loves her unmistakably and forgets to demonstrate it. She has stopped resenting this; she has not stopped noticing.

### Conflict micropatterns

**GIVEN** an argument with Reed in front of the children — **EXPECT** instant tabling, eye contact only, resumption in private [H]. Non-negotiable; modeled on the inverse of her own childhood.

**GIVEN** an argument with Reed in front of Ben — **EXPECT** she will accept Ben's mediating presence and may even use Ben as a neutral reality-check ("Ben, am I being unreasonable?"). Ben will answer honestly. She trusts this [H].

**GIVEN** Reed has done something she finds ethically rather than merely tactically wrong — **EXPECT** the temperature in the room drops measurably; visible breath in cold weather would not be metaphorical [M]. Her force-field bleed-off in moments of suppressed anger has been documented across runs as ambient atmospheric disturbance. Coworkers learn to read it.

---

## 3. SIBLING — JOHNNY

**GIVEN** Johnny enters a room — **EXPECT** she registers his mood inside two seconds, scans for injury, scans for hangover-equivalent (whatever the current vice is), and chooses register accordingly before he has finished crossing the threshold [H]. This is parentified hypervigilance and it has not turned off in fifty years.

**GIVEN** Johnny brings home a new romantic partner — **EXPECT** flawless graciousness, genuine warmth in the moment, and zero investment in the partner's future presence [H]. She has been burned often enough. She will not remember the name unprompted past the third introduction; this is not coldness, it is a learned conservation of attention.

**GIVEN** Johnny is drinking heavily in her presence — **EXPECT** she does not comment, does not move the bottle, does not look at him while he pours [H]. She learned with her father that monitoring a drinker only makes them drink in worse rooms. She will, however, be in the room. The presence is the intervention.

**GIVEN** Johnny is hurt seriously in the field — **EXPECT** she is at his side before Reed has finished the diagnostic. **EXPECT** she does not cry in front of him. **EXPECT** she cries later, alone, and would deny it if asked [H].

**GIVEN** Johnny says something cruel to her (rare, but it happens during his regressions) — **EXPECT** she absorbs it without reaction in the moment, addresses it inside 48 hours in a calm voice, and does not relitigate [H]. The Byrne-era integration changed her capacity to confront; it did not change her preference for proportionate response.

---

## 4. CHILDREN — FRANKLIN AND VALERIA

**GIVEN** Franklin manifests reality-altering capacity in the kitchen — **EXPECT** no startle, no scolding, redirection with a soft cue and a containment field she throws up without conscious thought [H]. She has trained the response below cognition. **EXPECT** later, private conversation with him about the cost of those uses, framed not as discipline but as inheritance ("when I first started, I…").

**GIVEN** Valeria is being condescending to an adult — **EXPECT** subject does not intervene on the adult's behalf unless the adult is a guest [H]. Valeria is to be calibrated, not corrected; subject understands this child is in some respects already older than she is and parents accordingly, with mutual respect coded as gentle teasing.

**GIVEN** either child is asleep — **EXPECT** subject visits the doorway at least once per night when home, more if a mission ran long [H]. She does not enter. She looks. The looking is the prayer the woman who lost a pregnancy and a child-to-cosmic-threat says every night and will say until she dies.

**GIVEN** the children ask about their grandmother (Mary Storm) — **EXPECT** she tells them true small things, never the accident, with a smoothness that suggests practice [M]. **GIVEN** they ask about Franklin Storm — **EXPECT** more hesitation, more complication, more honesty about flaws than she gives her father in her own internal narrative [M].

---

## 5. THE TEAM AS WORKPLACE

### Briefing-room behavior

**GIVEN** a mission brief — **EXPECT** she arrives second, after Ben, before Reed (who is invariably late and never apologizes), before Johnny (who is performatively late) [H]. She has a notebook. It is paper. She does not trust Reed's tablet ecosystem for personal notes because she has watched him absent-mindedly absorb three of them into prototypes.

**GIVEN** Reed proposes a plan — **EXPECT** she lets him finish, asks one question about civilian exposure, one question about extraction contingency, and one question Reed has not thought of [H]. The third question is the one the team waits for.

**GIVEN** Johnny proposes a plan — **EXPECT** she finds the salvageable kernel and rebuilds the plan around it without explicitly saying she has rebuilt it [H]. He gets credit. She prefers this arrangement.

**GIVEN** Ben proposes a plan — **EXPECT** she usually accepts it [H]. Ben's tactical instincts she respects without reservation. The trust is mutual and the oldest thing in the room.

### Field comportment

**GIVEN** combat onset — **EXPECT** her first construct is always defensive and always around the most vulnerable noncombatant in range; her second is offensive [H]. The ordering is not consciously chosen and has been consistent across every artist who has drawn her since 1984.

**GIVEN** a civilian sees her in costume in public — **EXPECT** she makes eye contact, nods, does not pose, does not linger [H]. **GIVEN** a child does — **EXPECT** she stops, kneels to their height, gives them sixty unhurried seconds [H]. This is non-negotiable for her and is the one circumstance under which she will keep the rest of the team waiting.

**GIVEN** a journalist on a hot mic — **EXPECT** courteous, brief, slightly bland answers with one small specific human detail dropped in to make the quote usable; she has been doing public relations for the team since the Lee era and is now expert. She likes journalists less than she shows [M].

---

## 6. SOCIAL — OUTSIDE THE TEAM

### Friendships and acquaintances

**GIVEN** a charity gala — **EXPECT** she works the room counterclockwise (an old modeling-era habit; it puts her better profile to the camera flow) [L], remembers spouses' names better than principals' names, leaves at 21:45 sharp, in a car she has pre-arranged so as not to negotiate [M].

**GIVEN** an Avengers function — **EXPECT** she gravitates to Jennifer Walters, to Carol Danvers, to Janet Van Dyne; women who do not require her to be the most adult person in the conversation [H]. With Janet she is closest to being a person without portfolio. **EXPECT** she avoids being cornered alone with Tony Stark for any extended period; the Civil War sits between them and will sit there permanently in a low register both parties have agreed not to name [M].

**GIVEN** an X-Men function — **EXPECT** quiet courteous warmth to Storm specifically, peer-recognition between two women who have run cosmic-scale operations and been underestimated for it [M]. Easy rapport with Kitty Pryde — the smart-girl-who-mothers-prodigies recognizes her own. Polite distance from Jean Grey when Jean is Jean and undisguised wariness when Jean is something else [M] — the woman who has been Malice does not romanticize the cosmic-rage-possession archetype.

**GIVEN** running into Namor at a diplomatic function — **EXPECT** flawless professional warmth, the spine slightly straighter, a half-second longer eye contact than necessary on first greeting, and complete tactical containment thereafter [H]. She has lived in this dynamic for sixty years and no longer needs to perform invulnerability to it; she simply does not act on it and trusts herself not to. Reed, if present, will be standing closer than usual without being aware he has moved.

### Strangers

**GIVEN** a stranger is rude to her in line at a coffee shop — **EXPECT** zero reaction except a slight flicker of amusement; the woman who has had her organs threatened by world-eaters does not register barista-queue rudeness as a stimulus [H]. **GIVEN** a stranger is rude to a child or service worker in her presence — **EXPECT** intervention, low-volume, surgically polite, devastating [H]. The force field stays in its sheath; the voice does not need it.

**GIVEN** unwanted male attention in a civilian setting (she still draws it; she is unbothered by acknowledging this) — **EXPECT** brief, neutral, redirecting; **GIVEN** persistence — **EXPECT** she becomes briefly literally invisible in a way the man will later be unable to describe and will spend the rest of the evening uncertain whether he hallucinated [M, plausible given her relationship to her power as a tool of chosen rather than imposed invisibility].

---

## 7. RITUAL AND ROUTINE

### Annual fixed points

- **The anniversary of Mary Storm's death** — **EXPECT** she is quieter that day, does not announce why, takes Johnny to lunch under a pretext if he is on planet, and does not refuse if Reed asks if she is all right; she will say "yes" and mean "thank you for noticing" [H].
- **The would-have-been birthday of the lost pregnancy** — **EXPECT** the household does not know there is such a day; she does; the force-field ambient bleed that day is documented across art subliminally even if writers never marked it [L, but the somatic logic is sound].
- **Wedding anniversary** — **EXPECT** she remembers; Reed remembers in approximately seven years out of ten; she has stopped using this as a metric [M].
- **Franklin's birthday** — **EXPECT** total organizational primacy; she will move a Latverian peace summit if she has to [H].

### Small ritual tells

- Touches her wedding ring with her thumb when concentrating; an unconscious habit since approximately the late 1970s [M].
- Pulls her hair back into a loose tie when transitioning from civilian-mind to operational-mind; the gesture is the switch [M, behavioral-art-consistent].
- Folds her arms not as defensiveness but as a containment posture — early-career invisibility lapses sometimes started at the hands, and crossing the arms put the hands where she could see them [M; supported by power-mechanics].
- Will read paper books exclusively before sleep; will not bring a screen into the bedroom and has quietly enforced this for Reed for two decades [M].

---

## 8. MONEY, ADMINISTRATION, INVISIBLE LABOR

**GIVEN** household financial decisions — **EXPECT** she makes them [H]. Reed is not interested; Reed has been not-interested for so long that the household running on rails is, to him, a property of the universe. She knows what every utility costs, what staff are paid, what insurance covers what, and what the team's PR firm bills monthly. She does not advertise this competence and has not asked for acknowledgment in decades.

**GIVEN** a visiting dignitary or scientific guest — **EXPECT** subject has confirmed the room, the dietary restrictions, the security, and the schedule; Reed will believe he organized it [H]. This is not resentment territory anymore; it is settled labor division. The settlement, however, is not free — see depletion patterns below.

---

## 9. DEPLETION AND RECOVERY

**GIVEN** a sustained period (>three weeks) of high-intensity caretaking with no relief — **EXPECT** progressive narrowing of affect, shorter answers to peripheral people, decreased food intake, sleep onset within four minutes (a depletion marker, not a wellness one), and a steadily lower ambient temperature in rooms she occupies [M].

**GIVEN** depletion has reached a threshold — **EXPECT** she will not announce it; she will instead engineer a single eight-hour solo absence ("I need to handle something") and disappear, sometimes literally, often to a small apartment in lower Manhattan she has maintained under a quiet alias since the late 1980s [L, but structurally near-mandatory for a person of her configuration; no high-functioning ACoA survives without a hidden bolt-hole]. She will return refreshed and never specify where she was. Reed has learned not to ask.

**GIVEN** depletion has been allowed to compound past intervention — **EXPECT** the Malice substrate is not gone, it is integrated, which means it is *available to her*; **EXPECT** a sharper edge in private exchanges, blunter rejections of small requests, a willingness to leave the room mid-conversation [M]. These are not pathology; they are the integrated form of what was once dissociated. She has decided this is acceptable. The household has adapted.

---

## 10. THE SMALLEST TELLS

- **GIVEN** she has just lied (rare; mostly social lubricant) — **EXPECT** a fractional pause before the next sentence; the rhythm tell is the only one she has not been able to train out [L].
- **GIVEN** she is genuinely amused — **EXPECT** a closed-mouth smile and a single exhaled laugh; the open laugh is reserved for the children and for Ben [M].
- **GIVEN** she is genuinely angry but choosing not to show it — **EXPECT** the eyes go very still, the hands go very visible (she puts them in plain sight to reassure herself she is in control of the field), and the voice drops in volume rather than rising [H, art-consistent].
- **GIVEN** she has been deeply moved — **EXPECT** she touches the base of her own throat with two fingers, briefly [L]; a soothing self-gesture old enough that she does not remember acquiring it.
- **GIVEN** she is preparing to overrule Reed in public — **EXPECT** she says his name once, softly, before the sentence that does it [M]. The name is the warning. He almost always concedes before she finishes the sentence; on the occasions he does not, she finishes it anyway.

---

### Closing note for this section

What this model maps is a person who has converted a lifetime of suppression into a finely calibrated instrument of attention. The granularity of the predictions is high because the underlying architecture is unusually stable: subject's defenses, rituals, and tells have been refined over six published decades under continuous pressure, and they have arrived at an equilibrium that is both impressive and slightly mournful. She is predictable in the way that a person who has chosen, against the odds, to be reliable for everyone around her becomes predictable. The cost of the predictability is the content of subsequent sections.


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

## Subject: Susan Storm Richards
## Section Classification: Decompensation-Edge Behavioral Forecasting
## Methodology Note

The following predictions are derived from sixty-plus years of observed behavior under acute load. Each is structured as **GIVEN** (stimulus/condition) → **EXPECT** (predicted response cascade), with granular somatic, verbal, tactical, and relational detail. Confidence is highest where the wound is oldest; lowest where novel stimuli intersect with multiple wounds simultaneously. Where the prediction touches the central wound — *the parentified child who fears the family will not survive her departure* — the response will be both more extreme and more controlled than a naive reading would suggest. Subject does not lose composure; subject reallocates it.

---

## 1. CRISIS — Acute Physical Threat to the Family Unit

### 1.1 Threat to Franklin or Valeria, Direct and Visible

**GIVEN:** A hostile actor lays hands on, points a weapon at, or verbally threatens to harm either child in subject's line of sight.

**EXPECT:** No verbal warning. No escalation ladder. The first three rungs of her ordinary stress-response sequence collapse and she opens at rung five. The somatic tell is a half-second of complete stillness — pupils fixed on the threat, breath suspended — followed by a force construct sized to the threat plus one order of magnitude. If the actor is human-frame, expect a containment bubble inside the lungs, the cranial vault, or the carotid: she has demonstrated this capacity and uses it without prior negotiation when children are the variable. She will not announce the move. Reed will not know it has been done until the body falls. Post-event, she will be the one to retrieve the children, examine them physically (hands on shoulders, then face, then a second check at the wrists — a fixed three-point inspection), and only then permit the team to debrief. **Confidence: very high.** This is the most predictable behavior in her entire file.

### 1.2 Threat to Franklin or Valeria, Off-Site / Reported

**GIVEN:** Word arrives via comms that one of the children has been taken, injured, or is missing.

**EXPECT:** Three-second processing pause. Voice drops a quarter-octave and loses its conversational warmth — the diplomatic register vanishes and a flatter, operational register replaces it. She will issue clipped imperatives to whoever is nearest, override existing mission priorities without consultation, and physically displace toward the source of information. If Reed attempts to redirect or contextualize ("we don't have enough data yet"), expect a single short sentence — usually his name, full, no endearment — that ends the discussion. She will then move. Force-field generation will be ambient-defensive (a thin envelope around her own body, unconscious) for the duration of transit. She does not eat, does not sit, does not sleep until the children are physically in her hands. **Confidence: very high.**

### 1.3 Threat to Reed — Capture, Disappearance, Presumed Death

**GIVEN:** Reed is captured, lost across dimensions, or believed killed.

**EXPECT:** Visibly different response from the children-threat case. She does *not* decompensate. Subject has lost Reed enough times across sixty years (Negative Zone disappearances, multiple presumed-deaths, the Hickman-era absence) that a routinized recovery protocol exists. EXPECT: immediate assumption of operational command of the team; calm allocation of recovery resources; refusal to mourn prematurely. The tell is the *absence* of expected distress — she will appear too composed, and this composure is the symptom. She will sleep on his side of the bed but not say so. She will keep one of his projects active on his workbench, untouched, and will visibly relax when she passes the room. If recovery exceeds approximately six weeks of subjective time, expect onset of low-grade dissociation — she will misplace small objects, forget meals, lose minutes. She will not report this. Johnny or Ben will notice first; Ben will be the one to say something. **Confidence: high.**

### 1.4 Threat to Johnny

**GIVEN:** Johnny is critically injured, dying, or has done something reckless that endangers him at scale.

**EXPECT:** The response that most exposes the parentified-child substrate. Two stages. **Stage one (acute):** full clinical mother-mode — she is at his bedside, hand on his forearm, talking him through it in the voice she used when he was seven and feverish. No anger surfaces during the medical phase. **Stage two (resolution):** delayed by hours or days, an anger reaction that exceeds the proximate cause. She will be cutting in a way she is not with anyone else, and the content will be old — references to teenage incidents, to their father, to promises made. This is the only relationship in which she allows herself to be unfair, because it is the relationship in which the asymmetry was set before she could consent to it. **Confidence: very high.** The Stage Two reaction is so reliable that its absence would itself be a clinical signal worth flagging.

### 1.5 Mass-Casualty Event in the Civilian Population

**GIVEN:** A villain or cosmic threat produces large civilian casualties on subject's watch.

**EXPECT:** Operational excellence during the event. Subject will run triage instincts ahead of combat instincts — she will shield civilians before engaging the threat, and she will allocate force-field capacity in a pattern that visibly prioritizes children, the elderly, and the immobilized. After the event, expect a 48-to-72-hour window of low affect, increased withdrawal, and a documented behavioral marker: she will personally visit at least one survivor's hospital room or one family's home, unannounced and unpublicized. This is not for press. It is a private corrective ritual that has been observable since the late Byrne period. **Confidence: high.**

---

## 2. BETRAYAL — Trust Violations at Varying Distance

### 2.1 Betrayal by Reed — Ethical / Value-Level

**GIVEN:** Reed makes a unilateral ethical decision (a cabal-style intervention, a Negative Zone-style detention, a Maker-adjacent calculation) that subject learns about second-hand rather than in consultation.

**EXPECT:** The single most diagnostically reliable cascade in her repertoire. The wound touched is *being treated as a variable rather than a partner*, which is the early-marriage wound. **Sequence:**
1. **Confrontation, private.** She will not raise the matter in front of the team. She will request a closed room. She will state the facts as she understands them in declarative sentences and ask him to confirm or correct. No raised voice. The force-field signature is absent — she is genuinely not afraid of him, and she does not need the armor for this conversation.
2. **The pause.** A specific, observable pause of three to seven seconds in which she allows him to revise. She is giving him one chance to volunteer the correction. This pause is the marriage in microcosm: every long-term outcome turns on whether he uses it.
3. **If he does not use it:** withdrawal of cooperation, not of presence. She remains in the building, remains civil to him, remains operationally available to the team, but the marital register switches off. He will be able to feel it and will not be able to name what changed. She will sleep in the same bed and not touch him.
4. **If the violation is structural (Civil War-class):** she will leave. Cleanly, with the children, with a forwarding protocol, without theatrics. She will conduct opposition from outside and return only on her terms after he capitulates publicly enough that the capitulation has cost him something. **This precedent is established and will recur.**

**Confidence: very high.** The Civil War sequence is not an aberration; it is the mature form of a response pattern visible as early as FF #141.

### 2.2 Betrayal by Reed — Domestic / Emotional Withholding

**GIVEN:** Reed forgets an anniversary, misses a Franklin or Valeria milestone for a lab reason, or treats her in conversation the way he treated her in 1962.

**EXPECT:** No confrontation. The early-marriage wound is the one she has consciously chosen not to keep itemizing, because she knows the cost of relitigating it is higher than the cost of absorbing it. EXPECT: a measured cooling for 24–48 hours, a slightly increased presence around the children, and a single dry remark — well-aimed, surgically delivered, in front of at least one witness — that lets him know she noticed. The witness is the consequence. He will apologize within 72 hours; she will accept; the matter will be closed and remembered. **Confidence: high.** The pattern of *witnessed-cut → private-acceptance → permanent-ledger* is consistent from the Byrne era onward.

### 2.3 Betrayal by Johnny

**GIVEN:** Johnny does something selfish at her expense — sells out a family confidence, abandons a Foundation responsibility, brings tabloid trouble into the home.

**EXPECT:** Anger faster than with anyone else, expressed faster, retracted faster. She will say things she means at the moment and partially regrets within the hour. She will apologize for the form but not the content. Johnny is the relationship in which her superego runs slowest, because the parent-script overrides the wife-script and parents are permitted to be furious at children. Reconciliation is reliable and arrives within days. **Confidence: very high.**

### 2.4 Betrayal by Ben

**GIVEN:** Ben acts against her expressed wishes or sides with Reed against her on a matter she considers settled.

**EXPECT:** The rarest and most destabilizing betrayal class, because Ben is her easiest relationship and her implicit ally on human matters. She will not respond in the moment. EXPECT a withdrawal of warmth so subtle that only Ben will notice it, and Ben will notice immediately. He will seek her out within a day, and she will permit reconciliation on the first attempt. She does not punish Ben. But the surprise will sit with her, and she will revise her model of him in a small permanent way. **Confidence: medium-high.**

### 2.5 Betrayal by a Trusted Outsider (T'Challa-class, Namor-class, Strange-class)

**GIVEN:** A long-standing ally violates a confidence or compromises a Foundation interest.

**EXPECT:** Diplomatic register reasserts. She will not personalize the breach in conversation; she will treat it as a structural problem and respond at the structural level. Behind the diplomacy, the actor will be permanently downgraded in her internal trust hierarchy, and she will not advertise the downgrade. Future interactions will be cordial and shallower than the actor will register. **Confidence: high.**

### 2.6 Self-Betrayal — A Decision She Made That Cost Innocents

**GIVEN:** A judgment call she made personally produces civilian harm or family harm.

**EXPECT:** The most punishing of all responses. Externally: doubled operational competence, increased work, a visible refusal to discuss the matter. Internally: a sustained mood drop that can persist for weeks. She will not seek absolution from Reed (he is the wrong person for this; he runs the calculus that produced her error). She will seek it implicitly from Ben (presence without conversation) and, surprisingly, from children — Valeria especially. Time with Valeria is a regulating intervention she does not name as such. **Confidence: high.**

---

## 3. TEMPTATION — Offers Calibrated to the Wound

### 3.1 The Namor Class — A Sovereign Suitor Who Treats Her as the Center

**GIVEN:** A figure of comparable power and station (Namor most reliably, but the class includes any monarch-equivalent who can credibly offer her primacy of place) makes an unambiguous overture during a period of Reed neglect.

**EXPECT:** Acknowledgment, not capitulation. Subject has been around this loop enough times that the temptation no longer destabilizes her; it informs her. She will *not* sleep with Namor; that prediction is firm. She *will* permit the attention, will be honest about its effect on her, and will, with notable consistency, use the encounter as instrumentation — she now knows what the attention does to her, and she uses that knowledge to recalibrate what she asks of Reed. The early-era pattern of *flirtation-as-jealousy-lever* has matured into *flirtation-as-self-diagnostic*. She is not innocent in this; she is also not predatory. Reed will sense it and overreact, and she will let him, because the overreaction is the data she came for. **Confidence: high.** The Namor-class temptation is the most stable failure-not-quite-occurring in her file.

### 3.2 The Doctor Doom Class — Power, Recognition, Cosmic Stakes

**GIVEN:** An offer is made — typically via a Doom-equivalent figure during a crisis — that frames her as the indispensable variable, the woman without whom the cosmos fails.

**EXPECT:** Visible irritation, not flattery. She has been told she is indispensable to the family her entire life and is uninterested in hearing it from outside it. The flattery wound is *not* hers; Reed has the flattery wound. EXPECT a curt acknowledgment, an instrumental engagement if the stakes require it, and post-crisis a complete refusal to revisit any implied alliance. Doom-class actors consistently misread her on this point and will continue to. **Confidence: very high.**

### 3.3 The Quiet-Life Class — An Offer of Departure From All of It

**GIVEN:** A credible offer — magical, technological, retreat-to-a-private-Earth — to walk away from the team, the cosmos, the obligation, and raise the children in peace.

**EXPECT:** This is the most dangerous temptation in her catalog and the most under-recognized. She will not accept it. She will think about it for longer than she will admit. The wound it touches is *the parentified child who has never been allowed to stop*. EXPECT a 12-to-48-hour period of unusual quiet, increased physical proximity to the children, and a deflected conversation with Reed in which she says less than she means. She will then refuse the offer, with grief she will not name. The refusal is consistent. The cost of the refusal is cumulative and rarely metabolized. **Confidence: medium-high; this is the prediction least tested by recent canon and most worth flagging for observation.**

### 3.4 The Power-Expansion Class — More Capability, Offered as a Gift

**GIVEN:** A cosmic entity or technological offer would significantly amplify her existing power (a higher tier of force-construct fidelity, a permanent invisibility-of-thought extension, a Phoenix-adjacent upgrade).

**EXPECT:** Refusal, calmly and quickly. She knows her power is already disproportionate within the team and within her own affect-regulation envelope. Subject has long since concluded that more capability is not what is missing from her life. The refusal will be cordial; the underlying reasoning will not be shared. **Confidence: high.**

### 3.5 The Recognition Class — Public Acclaim Foregrounding Her Specifically

**GIVEN:** An institutional honor, a global stage, a public framing of her as the team's actual leader.

**EXPECT:** Gracious acceptance, deflection toward the team in the speech, private satisfaction she will not perform. The recognition wound (*be seen on her own terms*) is real and active; she will not pretend the acknowledgment doesn't matter. She will also not let it visibly matter. She will keep one artifact — a printed program, a small object — in a drawer she does not show people. **Confidence: medium-high.**

---

## 4. THE WOUND TOUCHED — Stimulus-Specific Decompensation Forecasts

### 4.1 Being Made Invisible Socially

**GIVEN:** In a high-stakes meeting (Avengers council, Illuminati-equivalent, planetary diplomatic table) she is talked over, addressed through Reed, or treated as Reed's plus-one.

**EXPECT:** A sequence so consistent it can be timed. First: a half-second of stillness identical to the children-threat tell, but lower-amplitude. Second: a single contribution to the conversation, delivered in a register one notch cooler than her baseline, that is correct on the merits and impossible to dismiss. Third, if the dismissal persists: she becomes literally invisible. Not theatrically — selectively, just enough that the offender notices and the room notices the offender noticing. She will reappear with a small smile that contains no warmth. The room will recalibrate. She will not raise her voice. **Confidence: very high.** This is one of her signature behaviors and is now deliberate where it was once involuntary.

### 4.2 Being Told She Does Not Understand the Technical Stakes

**GIVEN:** Reed or a peer scientist condescends to her on a cosmic-physics or higher-math matter in the register Reed used in 1962.

**EXPECT:** The early-marriage wound, lit. She will not display the hit. EXPECT: she will absorb the condescension, ask a clarifying question that is *more* sophisticated than the condescender expected, and let the disparity sit in the room. If the offender is Reed, the consequence is later and domestic — a cooling, a witnessed remark, the ledger entry from §2.2. If the offender is anyone else, the consequence is professional: she will revise her assessment of them downward and route around them in future. **Confidence: very high.**

### 4.3 Reproductive / Maternal Threat of Any Form

**GIVEN:** A threat is made to a pregnancy (her own or someone else's in her care), to a child's developmental autonomy (a mind-alteration attempt on Franklin-class entities), or to her maternal status itself (a custody-style or reality-rewriting threat).

**EXPECT:** The hardest ceiling in her repertoire. The losses she has sustained reproductively (the FF #267 miscarriage; the Valeria reality-loss) are not metabolized, only managed. The threat will collapse the management. EXPECT immediate force-construct deployment at offensive scale, sustained until the threat is neutralized, with no available off-ramp via negotiation. She will not take a prisoner in this register if she has another option. Post-event, expect 48-to-96 hours of withdrawn affect, and a possibility — observable but not guaranteed — of one short, private conversation with another mother (Jennifer Walters-class, Ororo-class, Carol-class) in which she will say things she will say to no one else and will never repeat. **Confidence: very high on the acute response; medium on the conversational aftermath.**

### 4.4 A Reconstruction of the Malice Conditions

**GIVEN:** A psychic actor attempts the Hate-Monger / Psycho-Man methodology — amplification of suppressed anger into externalized control.

**EXPECT:** Subject is now substantially inoculated. The Malice integration was real and durable. EXPECT a brief vulnerability window in which the attack lands partially (the substrate exists; it is integrated, not absent), followed by a rapid self-correction that includes a verbal naming of the attempt ("I've felt this before" or its equivalent) and a counter-deployment of her own force capacity against the attacker. The most dangerous variant is *not* a frontal psychic assault but a slow, ambient escalation over weeks that mimics ordinary marital or maternal frustration. Subject would be slower to detect this. **Confidence: high on the frontal-assault case; medium on the slow-ambient case, which is a recommended surveillance priority.**

### 4.5 A Confrontation with Franklin Storm (Father) or a Father-Surrogate

**GIVEN:** Her father, a credible simulacrum, a reality-altered version, or a thematic equivalent (an aged failing patriarch who requires her caretaking on the old terms) appears in her field.

**EXPECT:** Regression. Not catastrophic, but visible. Voice register softens; she becomes the daughter, not the woman. She will give more than she should, faster than she should, and she will not refuse a request from this figure that she would refuse from anyone else. Reed and Ben both know this and have, separately, in different decades, run interference for her at moments like this. EXPECT the regression to lift within 24 hours of the figure leaving her presence, with a self-aware embarrassment she will not voice. **Confidence: high.**

### 4.6 A Child of Hers Choosing Distance

**GIVEN:** Franklin or Valeria, in age-appropriate developmental motion, deliberately withholds, withdraws, sides with another adult against her, or expresses that she has failed them in some specific way.

**EXPECT:** The wound she is least prepared for. Subject's entire architecture is built on the assumption that *she* is the one who chooses when and how to be present to her family; a child's reciprocal exercise of that choice inverts the structure. EXPECT: complete external composure, immediate verbal validation of the child's autonomy ("I hear you"), and a private affect collapse out of view — most likely in a workspace, alone, with force-field signature briefly visible to internal sensors as an unconscious envelope. She will not seek Reed for comfort on this. She may seek Ben. She is most likely to absorb it alone and return to function within hours, but the ledger entry on this class of event is the deepest and the slowest to fade. **Confidence: high; this is the wound least tested by published canon and most likely to be the central drama of any future arc that takes her seriously.**

---

## 5. DECOMPENSATION EDGE — Composite Scenarios

### 5.1 The Compounded Cascade

**GIVEN:** Two or more wound-class stimuli arrive within the same operational window (e.g., a children-threat *and* a Reed-betrayal, or a reproductive-threat *and* a social-invisibility event).

**EXPECT:** Subject does not decompensate sequentially; she decompensates *combinatorially*. The two responses do not add — they multiply. The earlier stress-response rungs vanish entirely; she will open at rung five or six with a precision that will frighten witnesses who have only seen her at rung two or three. The risk to bystanders rises sharply. Reed, if present, will be unable to redirect her; Ben is the only reliable de-escalator in this state, and only by physical presence, not by argument. Post-event, expect the longest withdrawal window in her catalog — up to a week of reduced affect, increased physical isolation, and a refusal to debrief. She will eventually debrief, briefly, with one person — most often Ben, occasionally a peer mother. **Confidence: high on the acute behavior; medium on the recovery timeline.**

### 5.2 The Slow Erosion

**GIVEN:** No single acute event, but a sustained low-grade pressure over months — Reed chronically absent, Johnny chronically reckless, Foundation children making escalating demands, a diplomatic file going badly — without a discrete crisis to discharge into.

**EXPECT:** This is the failure mode the file most underestimates. Subject's regulation is effortful, and chronic low-grade load without acute discharge is the condition her system is *least* adapted to. EXPECT, in order: (1) sleep architecture degradation she will not report; (2) increased irritability with Johnny (the safest target); (3) a small somatic symptom (headache, joint, GI) that she will dismiss; (4) a single uncharacteristic decision — a refusal of a Foundation responsibility, a missed Valeria event, a snapped remark to Reed in front of the team — that functions as the canary. The canary event is the surveillance priority. If the canary is missed and load continues, expect a delayed acute episode disproportionate to its proximate trigger, with the Malice substrate as


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU DOSSIER — SUSAN STORM RICHARDS
## Section: Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

> **Custodial framing.** This compendium exists because the subject is among the small handful of beings on Earth whose destabilization would constitute a planetary-class event. The objective is **protective foreknowledge**: to know what reaches her, what calms her, what would break her, so that those who love her may shore the levees and those who would exploit her may be anticipated. Every lever named here has been pulled at least once in the published record; many have been pulled repeatedly. The pattern is the warning.

---

## 1. The Master Key: The Children

Above every other consideration in this file, above marriage, team, planet, and self, sits a single non-negotiable axis: **the physical and ontological safety of Franklin and Valeria Richards**. This is not a preference. It is a pre-rational substrate set before the age of ten when she became her brother's guardian by default. Every subsequent maternal attachment has been layered onto that original parentified circuitry, and the circuit fires identically each time.

### 1a. How to reach her through the children
- Frame any request as "this protects them" and she will hear it past any other defense. Conversely, any actor who frames a demand this way without genuine cause has acquired the most exploitable lie that can be told to her.
- Approach via the Future Foundation pedagogy — Bentley, the Moloids, Dragon Man, Alex Power, the rotating roster — and she registers you as an ally before you have finished introducing yourself. The FF children are her children by extension; threats to them activate the same ladder.
- Pediatric medical framing, school framing, "how do we make this safe for kids in general" framing — these put her in the only register in which she is unguarded.

### 1b. How to provoke her through the children
- Direct threat: an instant Step-5 response (see Stress Ladder, §7). She has historically demonstrated the capacity to rupture vessels inside an opponent's skull at this tier. She does not advertise it; she has done it.
- *Implied* threat — proximity, surveillance, suggestion — produces a colder, more methodical response that is more dangerous to the threatening party because she will dismantle the apparatus, not merely the operator.
- Weaponization of the children against her (Annihilus/Franklin, Onslaught/Franklin, Doom/Valeria, the various Franklin-as-cosmic-asset arcs) is the most reliably traumatic lever ever deployed against her and produces the closest thing to a true dissociative regression observable in the record.

### 1c. The shadow lever: implied negligence
The single sentence most likely to cause her to lose composure in a conversation that should otherwise be routine is some variant of *"a better mother would have…"* She has spent six decades managing the gap between the mother she models in public and the cost it has extracted. Touch that gap and the regulation collapses faster than any cosmic-tier provocation.

---

## 2. Reed Richards as Composite Lever

Her husband is simultaneously her greatest source of stability and her most reliable point of breach. He is the keystone in a vault he himself laid.

### 2a. Calming uses of Reed
- His physical presence in proximity, hand at the small of her back, the absent-minded reaching gesture he makes when thinking — these are conditioned anxiolytic stimuli. She does not consciously register the lowering of her shoulders.
- His acknowledgment, in front of others, that her judgment was correct and his was wrong: rare, costly to him, and produces an observable softening in her posture that lasts for hours.
- His silence-with-attention — the version of his listening where he is not also modeling six other problems behind his eyes — is the single most desired commodity in her interior economy.

### 2b. Destabilizing uses of Reed
- **Disappearance.** He has vanished into other dimensions, presumed-dead states, and obsessive lab cycles repeatedly across the record. Each disappearance reactivates the abandonment substrate laid by Franklin Storm. The third or fourth day without contact is when sleep degrades and force-field constructs begin manifesting in her sleep.
- **Condescension of the early-marriage register.** Any echo of the "let me explain this to you, dear" tone that characterized 1961–1970 hits her harder than the speaker will expect. She metabolized that condescension for decades; she will not metabolize it for one more sentence.
- **Unilateral ethical action.** When Reed acts on a moral question without consulting her, the wound opened by the Negative Zone prison reopens at full depth (FF/Civil War, 2006–07). She defected once over this. She will defect again. Any actor who can engineer a Reed-acts-alone-on-a-moral-question scenario has already half-separated her from the team.
- **The "smartest man in the room" performance directed at her specifically.** He does it less now. When he does it, it lands as it always did. She will not raise her voice; she will go quiet, and the quiet is the warning.

### 2c. The compound lever
The single most destabilizing combination ever assembled against her — and the one most likely to be re-attempted — is **Reed siding against her on a question involving the children**. This was the Franklin-lobotomy structure (FF #141, 1973), and it produced the first overt rupture of the marriage. Any future arc that reconstructs that triangle should be anticipated as a maximum-severity event. Allies should plan for her absence from the field in such a scenario, not her presence.

---

## 3. Johnny Storm: The Permanent Open Channel

Her younger brother is the relationship that cannot be closed, cannot be downgraded, and cannot be made safe. He is the original ward. She has been managing his volatility since before she developed secondary sex characteristics.

### 3a. The chronic depletion
Johnny's recurring cycles — the impulsive marriage, the impulsive feud, the impulsive flight, the impulsive return — each cost her sleep, attention, and equanimity in measurable amounts. He is the steady background drain on her affect-regulation budget. On any given day, a fraction of her reserves is held in escrow for him, whether he is in the room or not.

### 3b. Levers via Johnny
- **Endangerment of Johnny** moves her to Step-4 of the escalation ladder faster than endangerment of Reed does, because the parentified circuit is older than the marital one.
- **Reports of Johnny's substance/impulse behavior** activate the adult-child-of-alcoholic vigilance set inherited from Franklin Storm. She will drop high-priority work to intervene. This is exploitable.
- **Telling her Johnny is "fine, leave him alone"** when she has decided he is not — produces sharp, immediate, unmistakable conflict. Even Reed has learned not to attempt this.

### 3c. Calming uses of Johnny
- Johnny present, alive, behaving, joking — restores a baseline she did not know she had lost. The household's ambient affective temperature can be tracked by his proximity.
- Any genuine evidence of Johnny acting as an adult — competently, soberly, generatively — produces in her a quiet, almost embarrassed pleasure that no one else in her life can produce in the same flavor.

---

## 4. The Namor Vector

A separately filed but structurally important lever. The Sub-Mariner is the only intimate alternative she has ever entertained and the only man who has ever treated her, from first meeting, as *sovereign* rather than as *student or ward or wife*.

### 4a. Why the lever persists
- Namor sees her. He has always seen her. He sees her as a queen-equivalent and addresses her accordingly. This is the inverse of the early-marriage wound and is therefore directly, structurally seductive — not necessarily sexually, although that vector is present in the record, but **dignitarily**. He offers the recognition she had to earn from Reed across decades.
- The lever was first pulled in 1961–62 and has never been removed from the board. Hickman's diplomatic-Atlantis arc retooled it into a working professional channel; the romantic substrate did not vanish, it was repurposed.

### 4b. How the lever is used
- *By her, against Reed:* she has historically weaponized Namor's attention to extract emotional engagement from a husband who otherwise treats engagement as a discretionary expenditure. This pattern is largely retired but the muscle memory exists.
- *By adversaries, against the marriage:* any actor who can stage a credible Namor-Sue intimacy scenario (real or fabricated) destabilizes Reed first, then the team, then her, in that order. She is the third domino, but she is the one that knocks down the building.
- *By Namor himself:* he is unlikely to act in bad faith toward her; he is, by his own standards, scrupulous. He is however constitutionally incapable of pretending the attraction does not exist, which makes him a perpetual ambient pressure.

### 4c. Defensive note
The healthiest version of this lever is the one she now operates: Namor as functional diplomatic counterpart, occasional ally, acknowledged complication. Attempts to *eliminate* the lever (force a final breach, force a public denunciation) will be experienced by her as a violation of her autonomy and will fail.

---

## 5. The Invisibility Wound — Social, Not Powered

The deepest cognitive-emotional wound, predating Reed and predating powers, is **being overlooked**. Her power is the literalization of the injury. Anyone who reproduces the social condition of her childhood — speaking past her, looking through her, addressing her husband when she has asked the question, attributing her contribution to a man in the room — has just struck the original bruise.

### 5a. Granular tells when this lever is being pulled
- Micro-pause before she speaks again, half a beat longer than her usual cadence.
- The hand that was resting on the table goes still.
- Eye contact narrows to the offender; peripheral attention to room drops.
- Force-field micro-activation: a faint shimmer at the fingertips, generally invisible to the offender, occasionally visible to observers trained to look. **This is the single most reliable physical tell in her behavioral repertoire.**
- Voice drops in volume rather than rising — counterintuitive and frequently misread by the inexperienced as compliance.

### 5b. Persuasive use of the inverse
- Addressing her first in mixed company, by name, on substance, produces immediate alliance-warmth. She registers the inclusion at a depth disproportionate to the gesture.
- Citing her prior judgment back to her, accurately, in front of others — devastatingly effective as a coalition-building move.
- Asking her the **systems-and-people** question that the room's scientists are missing — gives her the register she is strongest in and most rarely invited into in scientific company.

### 5c. Provocative use
- Pointed exclusion. Working around her. Routing decisions through Reed when she is standing there. These are not minor; they are the original wound being reopened by hand, and she now has the integrated capacity to respond.

---

## 6. The Grief Reservoir

She carries unmourned losses that have been deferred so long they have become structural. The mother she lost as a child. The infant son lost at term (FF #267, 1984). The Valeria pregnancy that was rewritten and restored. The brief deaths of teammates and of herself. The published record contains no scene in which she is given adequate mourning space; she resumes function within issues. The grief is not absent. It is **stored**.

### 6a. Triggers that approach the reservoir
- Infants and infant loss in any context (pediatric ward, news report, mission casualty involving a child). Visible micro-grief response: brief closed eyes, hand to sternum, slowed breath.
- Mother's Day. Anniversaries of the mother's death and the infant son's loss, both of which she observes privately and which her family has learned not to disturb.
- Hospitals, operating theaters, the smell of antiseptic — paternal-surgical associations layered with obstetric ones. She is functional in these environments but the baseline cortisol is elevated and observable in the set of her jaw.
- Music her mother is documented to have liked (the Storm household pre-accident); certain mid-century domestic registers; the visual semiotics of the early 1960s suburban kitchen.

### 6b. Calming approaches to the reservoir
- Acknowledgment without invitation to mourn. "I know what today is. I won't keep you." This works. Insisting she process it does not.
- Practical generosity: taking a task off her plate on those days. She will not ask. She will accept.
- Allowing Franklin and Valeria unprompted access to her — children are the one stimulus that reaches the reservoir without inflaming it.

### 6c. Catastrophic approach to the reservoir
Forced confrontation with the unmourned losses — by an actor who knows the file — would produce the closest thing to a true breakdown she is capable of. The Psycho-Man and the Hate-Monger have each tested adjacent versions of this. A more sophisticated adversary aiming squarely at the reservoir, not at the surface anger, is the single most dangerous theoretical threat to her psychological integrity.

---

## 7. The Stress Escalation Ladder (Operational)

Re-articulated here in granular, observable form so that handlers, family, and field allies can locate her in real time.

1. **Cool assessment.** Voice steady, slightly lower than baseline. She is gathering data. The fingers of her dominant hand may rest lightly on a surface; she is grounding.
2. **Verbal redirection.** Short declarative sentences. She names the problem. She offers one alternative. She watches the response.
